Current Commentary

The Maturation of the Greek Restoration Movement 11

— Ang

General Theodoros Kolokotronis, a leader of the 19th-century Greek independence movement, once said, "Greece cannot survive without a monarch." The current Greek statesman Panagis Tsaldaris was one of the drafters of the 1924 Geneva Protocol and is currently the ambassador to France. He recently also served as an arbitrator for the Arbitral Tribunal. In an opinion published in an Athens newspaper, he also stated, "A constitutional monarchy is far superior to a democratic autocracy." It can be seen that the Greek nation's inclination towards the imperial system is deep and long-standing. This restoration movement, within the ruling class, has been carefully arranged for a long time. The referendum held on the 3rd under military control was merely a formality. According to recent dispatches, the total vote count showed that those in favor of restoring the imperial system numbered 1,501,992 votes against 33,360 votes, accounting for the vast majority. It is indeed what was expected.

The Greek Republic was declared on May 1, 1925. This revolution was in fact a result of the defeat in the Asia Minor Campaign. After the European War, Greece, supported by the Allied forces of Britain and France, attempted to annex Smyrna, which it had coveted for a long time. However, due to the heroic resistance of the Turkish national hero Kemal Atatürk, it suffered a major defeat in Asia Minor. Subsequently, domestic coups followed one after another. King Constantine was forced to abdicate for the second time on January 11, 1923. George II succeeded him, but was soon deposed by the parliament on December 17 of the same year. On March 25, 1925, the parliament passed a resolution to overthrow the imperial system and establish a republic. On April 13, a national referendum approved the change of system with 758,742 votes against 325,322 votes. The official announcement of the change of system was made on May 1, and it has been only ten and a half years since then.

There are three major political parties in Greece, namely the Republican Party, the Imperial Party, and the Social Communist Party. The Republican Party is led by Eleftherios Venizelos and is based on the island of Crete. Venizelos is one of the great modern Greek politicians, having guided Greek affairs for twenty years. The current Kontylis, who is most strongly advocating for the restoration, was originally also affiliated with the Republican Party. The Imperial Party is divided into extremist and moderate factions. The former Prime Minister Tsaldaris is the leader of the moderate faction. The Republican Party also has considerable influence in the army and navy. Seeing the imperial trend becoming more and more intensified, they joined forces with the Social Communists on March 1 of this year to launch an uprising to make a final defense of the republican system. However, it was only a flash in the pan, and Eleftherios Venizelos, in his declining years, fled to Paris. After this, Kontylis very much wanted to restore the monarchy in one fell swoop. However, Tsaldaris, as Prime Minister, was unwilling to act rashly on the change of the national system. George II was also quite cautious about his own position. Therefore, even after the two political upheavals of July 19 and October 10, Kontylis still had to decide this important political system issue through a public referendum. Now that the results of the referendum are like this, the Imperial Party can get what they want.

However, this small country with a population of 6.6 million has had several cases of its monarchs being deposed and assassinated in the past hundred years, according to historical records. Since the collapse of the imperial system in 1924, the intensity of party strife has also been constantly reported. It can be seen that whether it is an imperial system or a democracy, it is difficult for Greece to achieve long-term stability and security. Moreover, the power of the Eleftherios Venizelos faction still has residual strength to be exploited, and George II, who is currently residing in London, even among those in the Imperial Party, may have disagreements about his return to power.

Political Situation Unlikely to Change Before Greek King Returns Home; No Politicians Allowed to Take Advantage of the Opportunity for Selfish Gain 12

Athens After the results of the Greek referendum determined support for the restoration, political figures here believe that the political situation is unlikely to change before King George returns from England. Former Prime Minister Tsaldaris, leader of the People's Party, recently issued a declaration stating that although the people have voted in favor of the restoration, politicians are not allowed to use the opportunity to pursue their own selfish gains. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Athens It was officially announced here today that the total vote on Sunday showed 1,501,992 votes in favor of a constitutional monarchy and 33,360 votes against. General Kondylis, the Regent, today had the Greek cabinet swear allegiance in the name of George II. George II will soon return from London to ascend the throne. (4th National Telegram)

Athens King George recently issued a proclamation to the Greek people from England, stating, "By divine decree and the will of the people, I have resumed the throne. From now on, I shall take the national constitution as my guide. I hope that all levels of the nation will work together to make our motherland prosperous and happy." Also, news has it that King George will return home via Yugoslavia. (5th Havas Dispatch)

(Vienna) After the news of the Greek referendum results, which showed a majority in favor of the former king's restoration, reached here, the Austrian Imperial Party unanimously rejoiced. They feel that they will soon be able to force former Prime Minister Starhemberg to clearly express his opinion on the restoration of Archduke Otto. Fischer, who was recently squeezed out by Starhemberg, delivered a speech to 8,000 imperialists today, demanding that the Habsburg imperial family return home as soon as possible. (4th National Telegram)

Border Conflict Incident; Russian Ambassador Refutes Japanese Dispatch, Accusing Japanese and Puppet Troops of Provoking Across the Border 13

(Moscow) The Russian ambassador to Japan today sent a note to Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota, stating that the Japanese claim that the border incidents on October 6 and 12 were caused by illegal activities of Soviet border guards is completely unfounded, and claiming that Japanese "Manchu" mixed troops illegally invaded Russian territory and attacked Russian troops, causing the conflict. The Russian and Japanese sides have different opinions on this conflict. After the incident occurred, the Russian authorities immediately protested, claiming that 50 Japanese and Manchu troops crossed the border at Grodekovo, near Khabarovsk, and opened fire on Russian soldiers, who then returned fire, resulting in several deaths and injuries. According to the Japanese explanation, on October 6, 15 miles west of Nov Alekseevskoye, a Manchu infantry patrol encountered six Russian cavalrymen in Manchu territory. The Russian cavalrymen refused to be questioned and opened fire, and the Manchu troops returned fire. The Russian cavalrymen then retreated, and the Manchu troops chased them to the border, seizing a horse. They then inspected the area and found that the Russian side had built a temporary bridge to facilitate the movement of their cavalry. On October 12, the Manchu side sent some soldiers to investigate. At 3 p.m. that day, they encountered 50 Russian cavalrymen with machine guns and bombs in the area. The Russian cavalrymen also opened fire, attempting to surround the Manchu troops. The two sides therefore fought each other, but the number of deaths and injuries is still unknown. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

The Italian Offensive in the Northern Front Suddenly Comes to a Halt 14

Heavy Rain Makes Military Operations Difficult; Twenty-One Mules Have Difficulty Pulling One Cannon; Italy Implements Austerity Measures

(Rome) Today, the authorities here announced that the general offensive that began on Sunday on the entire northern front has now stopped to complete the construction of the roads. It is reported that the Italian First Army Corps, which advanced from Maruk yesterday, has now reached the territory of Meaine and occupied the village of Adibahei. Two columns of Italian troops and native legions are said to have occupied Hoshan, and another column has set off from the Danakil lowlands and advanced to the Dagu River basin, occupying the eastern defenses of Agam. A telegram received today from Asmara stated that the Italian troops in the northern front are currently holding and controlling the lines of communication to the mountain valleys of Agra and Suro. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Asmara The Italian troops in the northern front have now advanced to a location 20 miles from Mek'ele. It is expected that after the vanguard troops occupy their destination tonight, they will wait for the arrival of the main forces and set up a new alert formation, which will be 40 to 50 miles further than the Adowa line. It is not the rainy season now, but the weather is abnormal, with continuous rain for days. The Italian troops have to advance in the rain. The mud is terrible, and the difficulty of the march can be imagined. In one place, 21 mules were not enough to drag a cannon over the rocks. The forward commanders of the Italian army are now afraid that the rain will wash away the military road behind them, causing the forward troops to be disconnected from the Adowa headquarters. Air reconnaissance reports that the Ethiopian troops have turned south, which proves that they do not want to resist the Italian army at this time. Therefore, based on the current situation, a major battle is unlikely to occur this month. The troops in the Danakil front are now advancing rapidly to the south and have been in contact with the rear, so there is no danger of an isolated force deep in the enemy's territory. (5th National Telegram)

(Rome) Italy is currently carrying out a plan to weaken the effects of League of Nations sanctions. Today, the Fascist Party conference officially decided to encourage rabbit breeding to increase meat supply. The authorities are also collecting scrap iron throughout the country. Trains have reduced their mileage by 6,000 miles per day to save fuel. At the same time, pilots who participated in the 1934 International Air Race have handed over their gold medals to the state for melting. British and American residents in Italy are now sending their families out of the country in droves to prevent food shortages and Italian xenophobia. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

(Rome) The Italian government, in order to resist sanctions, has issued an order to the whole country to save consumption. All domestic butcher shops will be closed for the first time today, and it has been decided to close one day per week from now on. In addition, all hotels and dining cars will limit meals to one dish. (5th Havas Dispatch)

(Rome) Although those responsible in Addis Ababa claim that the Ethiopian troops will defend the city of Mek'ele to the last man, people here all believe that the city will fall soon. The Italian troops currently attacking Mek'ele total at least three armies. One army is attacking head-on from Adigrat, and the remaining two armies are advancing from the holy cities of Adowa and Aksum, both from the southwest. A column of the First Army Corps, commanded by General Santini, has advanced to Agula, about 15 miles from Mek'ele, with its outposts stationed on the other side of the valley that almost overlooks Mek'ele. Heavy rain fell at night, turning the roads near Mek'ele into a mire. At the same time, the main target of the Italian troops in the southern front, Harar, initially appeared to be the site of a major battle last night, but according to reliable frontline news, the Italian troops' fierce attack has not yet begun, but is imminent. It is widely believed that the large army commanded by General Graziani now has Gorahei as its target. According to unofficial sources, the army has about 50 tanks to assist in the battle. Although the Ethiopian troops have dug trenches near Gorahei to defend themselves, it is feared that it will be difficult to withstand the combined attack of tanks, planes, and infantry. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Addis Ababa Our special correspondent Ouchena reports that Italian troops have been bombing the town of Gorahei for days with planes. The town is an important town in the Wardagai region, rich in water sources, and is also a major transportation hub. Therefore, many civilians in the town have been killed and injured by bombs. There are very few Ethiopian troops stationed in Gorahei town. The Ethiopian government is very puzzled as to what the purpose is of Italian planes repeatedly bombing the town. Some people believe that the Italian troops' target may be the Ethiopian residents. Also, the Italian troops have resumed their attack on the city of Mek'ele on the northern front. No news has been received here, but it is heard that native soldiers from Italian Eritrea are still fleeing in large numbers. Therefore, the strength of the troops led by General Wondirad, the Commander-in-Chief of Tigray Province, who are currently stationed south of Adowa, has greatly increased. (4th Havas Dispatch)

(Rome) A dispatch from the Italian front today stated that Italian bombers bombed the enemy army in advance and discovered 10,000 Ethiopian troops advancing north towards Mek'ele. As the Italian troops advanced south, they encountered resistance along the way and have now occupied most of the villages. Observers today generally believe that after occupying their destination, the Italian troops will need about a month to reorganize their defenses before launching another attack. Baldwin's Speech: Europe Needs British Assistance; Collective System Opens a Bright Path 21

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin recently delivered a campaign speech to over 5,000 people, discussing domestic affairs and economic policies, and paying particular attention to the cotton weaving industry in Lancashire and the Liverpool port commerce. Finally, he mentioned foreign affairs and defended the policies adopted by the government, saying, "We ask the people to trust us so that we can continue our work and be creators of a new Britain. If God blesses us, we also hope to reform Europe. My political opponents accuse the government of being self-satisfied with all its measures. It must be known that the government is not like this. We have a very deep understanding of the responsibilities we bear and the responsibilities that our political opponents avoid. I dare say that our work has had good plans from the beginning, and I hope that future achievements can also be comparable." Baldwin also said, "What Europe needs is a strong and experienced British government so that it can assist other governments when necessary. However, there is a pleasing thing now, that is, the League of Nations can deal with major events that stimulate world opinion in a lively and vigorous manner, making those who intend to destroy it discouraged and opening a bright future for the collective security system. I believe that there is indeed a strong and firm desire for peace in Europe. This can be seen in the fact that the League of Nations Adjustment Committee passed a proposal without our initiative, entrusting Britain and France to do their best to mediate the Italian-Ethiopian dispute in order to find a solution that can satisfy the League of Nations and Italy. Even if we cannot eliminate the war before it happens, we should not be afraid of difficulties and end the war as soon as possible. This solution should be within the scope of the League of Nations. If it can be found, all human beings will be honored. All member states should have this feeling, and how can our Britain be outside of this?" (5th Havas Dispatch)

Words on Locusts' Backs Indicate a World War is Coming 32

This omen appeared before the Spanish-American War and World War I.

Strange discovery by American veterans

World Society, Bristol (Oklahoma, USA) - According to Edward Maurice, a veteran of the Spanish-American War who is now a local resident, a world war will soon break out. His reason is that locusts have recently been found in the local countryside with the English letter "W" naturally formed on their backs, which is an abbreviation for "War". He said that he had seen locusts with the same appearance on their backs before the Spanish-American War and World War I. He also said that if there was only one "W", it would not be so bad, but unfortunately there is a small circle below the letter, which indicates that the war will spread throughout the world.

Berlin Correspondence

The Attitude of the Italian People Towards the East African War 33

— Zhang Tiesheng

The Italian Blackshirt Prime Minister Mussolini once roared like a lion: "I would rather be a lion for one day than a sheep for a hundred years." Therefore, he disregards everything and desperately "ventures" into Africa. On the surface, he takes "civilizing the black race" as his responsibility, but in reality he "wants to turn Abyssinia into Italy's Morocco." In this way, he can not only enable three million Italians to immigrate to Africa, but also extend the work of Italians civilizing blacks for at least fifty years.

Do the British want to sanction the Italians? "The meaning of sanctions is war," is Gada's reply. Do the British want to block the Suez Canal? "Italy will resist them with all its might on land, sea, and air," is Mussolini's reply. The recent meeting of the Italian cabinet in Bolsano also took the same stance.

We can get a glimpse of the Italian authorities' attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian War from this. But what is the attitude of the Italian people? This is also a question that we must pay attention to. Naturally, we cannot find a real answer to this question in the Italian newspapers.

No matter who it is, if he stays in Italy for a while, he will find that the issue that Italians are most concerned about is the "Abyssinian War." Most of them express disapproval of the war. They hold the view of abhorring war, and many people even think that it is suicide. But there is no public opposition, because Fascism's thirteen years of dictatorial rule has made them afraid to oppose it through obvious or implicit policies of terror.

Of course, nationalism is not without effect among Italians. However, those who embrace nationalism believe that there are other ways to seize "a place in the sun" besides war. Even within the Fascist Party, there are those who criticize it. For the sake of caution, they naturally do not dare to criticize it publicly, but their disapproval or disguised criticism inevitably shows in their expressions. Many capitalists initially had some delusions about the situation of frantic war preparations, but since Mussolini announced that he would levy heavy taxes on them during the military parade in Bolsano, their excitement has been chilled to zero. The upper middle class also frowns and is even resentful, but there is nothing they can do. The only reason they have always helped Fascism is because it is the only savior to resist communism, but now the exorbitant taxes, heavy levies, and the depression of business and the gloom of the future have made them lose hope. However, they have to continue to help, because they know that if the current government collapses, it will immediately become a state of anarchy, or even become the world of the Communist Party. What they are most worried about is that if Italy's war with Abyssinia fails, Fascism will inevitably disintegrate; but the aftermath of the disintegration is unimaginable.

One Fascist said this: "Young people are wholeheartedly Fascists. They don't know anything else, but I am over fifty years old, I am both a Fascist and a complete nationalist; but we old people are not accustomed to the dangers caused by Fascism in its undertakings. I don't know what will happen to me and my family when I am old." From this, it can be seen that Mussolini's roar: "Venture!" is not even able to agitate his followers above a certain age. Those who once helped him seize power are mostly eager to live a "happy old age" and are unwilling to continue taking desperate risks. In the workers of northern and southern Italy, more than half have definitely not been subdued by Fascism. Even members of the Fascist labor union do not necessarily support the Fascist regime. They are only forced to join for economic reasons, so their attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian War is conceivable. But Mussolini may pay extra attention to them, because he used to be a socialist himself. He knows the importance of workers and cannot let them become desperate people. Although he thinks so, the workers definitely do not like Fascism. The workers who express support on the surface are only doing it for their own jobs. Especially those workers who participated in World War I or other wars are all the more in favor of peace. There are even those who openly oppose the war.

Not only are the workers in Italy like this, but even the General Staff of the Roman Army has opposed venturing into Abyssinia, which is now an open secret. The army, whose profession is being soldiers, also believes that this kind of venture is an extremely risky deal, considering the economic, financial and other practical aspects. It goes without saying that the troops who have already gone to Africa complain, and even the troops who have not yet left feel that the future is bleak. As for the news of wanting to avoid military service, we hear it even more often.

Even among Fascists in high positions, there are a few who opposed the venture from the beginning. However, although the General Staff also opposes it, they are all from the military and only know how to obey. They know that this venture is tantamount to gambling, but they have to support it. Regarding the attitude of the Italian Emperor, rumors also say that he opposes the war. However, Mussolini's methods are after all very strong. He does not want to bear the responsibility for the war alone. At the same time, he also makes the royal family share the responsibility for all war plans, because he tries his best to make many members of the royal family occupy the leading positions in the war. In this way, once there is an accident, he can very well push the blame on them.

I have already said above that there is no public opposition to the Italian-Abyssinian War among Italians. When they talk about this issue, they are very careful and cautious, fearing disaster. They are even unwilling to discuss this issue with a foreigner, fearing that he is a detective of the Fascists. A reporter from a certain newspaper heard three middle-aged businessmen in Milan talking about the war. They all opposed the war because prices had been raised too high and would continue to rise. Even daily commodities are difficult to sell, let alone the luxury goods that are still being manufactured in large quantities in northern Italy. Whether it is salaries or wages, they are constantly being drastically reduced. As the purchasing power of Italians decreases, and at the same time taxes increase, the general lack of prosperity in commerce is a natural result. Furthermore, Italians are now openly opposing price increases. A Fascist wanted to buy an orange on a hot day, and the seller asked for two lira. "This is a price for selling to the British, not for selling to Italians," he said angrily.

In many villages in Italy, the attitude of opposing the war, due to government suppression, can mostly only be written in chalk on the walls on both sides of the streets. In the narrow lanes of Venice and Genoa, in the small streets of Naples, the walls are full of slogans against the war. Slogans supporting the war by the Fascists are immediately painted over.

However, Fascism's thirteen years of terror policies have after all eradicated all public opposition. No matter what the Italians write on the walls, it is of no use in reality. This is why Mussolini is able to disregard everything and do whatever he wants. He has not only been doing whatever he wants for thirteen years, but he also wants to continue doing so, and at the same time he feels that he is able to do so, because he is still obviously a ruler of Italy. As for the future hidden dangers caused by the Italian-Abyssinian War, he has not paid much attention to them.

Now, any expression of opposition to the war in Italy is of course weak. Mussolini now of course has wholehearted young people behind him (because they have all been educated by the Fascists for thirteen years and do not know anything else), but the speculative deal of the Italian-Abyssinian War not only hides future hidden dangers in the country, but also creates a formidable enemy abroad. (Sent on October 2)

After the Promulgation of the New Currency System, Financial Stability in Various Regions 34

There are occasional instances of rising prices, but no disruptions or impacts on the market.

(Beiping) The Ping silver circles have largely determined a method for dealing with the centralized silver cash. First, they will statistically account for the amount of silver deposits and silver notes. Then, they will determine how to handle the silver cash, how to redeem silver cash with legal tender, and the methods for commercial bank notes. The issue of redeeming silver cash on the market is relatively simple, because in recent years, too much silver has flowed out of the Ping market, leaving very little. Apart from the silver firms, the amount of silver scattered among the citizens is minimal, so redemption will not be a problem. The steps determined by the association are that each bank will separately engage in internal statistics. At the same time, they will telegraph the Ministry of Finance and the three major banks, the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, to request instructions on everything. After the above work is completed in a day or two, another general meeting will be held to decide on the methods for redeeming silver cash and commercial bank silver notes with legal tender, and then announced for implementation. (5th Dispatch)

(Beiping) After the price of copper coins in the Ping market soared a few days ago, the prices of general merchandise also surged. In the past two days, each bag of white flour has risen by six or seven dimes, and each dan of rice has also surged by one yuan and several dimes. (5th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Silver Guild held a meeting on the 4th, and elected Bian Baimei, the head of the Bank of China, as chairman. Representatives from 23 banks and money houses attended. It was resolved that (1) the silver and money industries would uniformly comply with the government's methods for consolidating the currency system; (2) transfers among Tianjin counterparts would continue to be handled by the public treasury, and all payments would be made with the notes of the three banks. The silver cash stored in the public treasury would be sealed by the two guilds and the three banks according to the inventory on the 2nd; (3) from the 4th onward, all checks issued by the banks and money houses would be written in national currency. Previously issued checks and checks issued after the 4th that have the words "current silver dollar," "silver dollar," or "silver ocean" written on them would all be treated as national currency and paid in the notes of the three banks. The silver and money guilds have telegraphed silver and money counterparts in various places to inform customers and explain any doubts they may have. (4th Dispatch)

(Zhenjiang) Since the Ministry of Finance announced the currency decree, all industries in Zhenjiang have decided to comply. However, merchants are arbitrarily raising prices and lowering the price of foreign currency, so that the exchange rate of each yuan has fallen from 3,400 wen to 2,800 or 2,900 wen. It is now known that the business conditions of various industries will follow the Shanghai standard. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Because the Ministry of Finance is implementing the policy of consolidating the currency system, and the market is nervous, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened a temporary emergency meeting this morning and resolved: (1) to issue a public notice to advise merchants and citizens to earnestly abide by the laws and regulations and not to raise prices under any pretext; (2) to compile and print a notice to be distributed to citizens; (3) to schedule a joint meeting of various trade associations on the afternoon of November 6th; (4) regarding the issue of replenishing funds, to send a letter to the Silver Guild to earnestly discuss revitalizing the market; (5) to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to support the new policy of reforming the currency system, and to promptly implement the mortgage law for real estate, so as to implement it as soon as possible in order to further consolidate the effectiveness of the currency system, rescue the market, and revive the countryside. (5th Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications have shipped one million yuan of legal tender banknotes from Shanghai to circulate in the market. The financial situation is quite stable, and the opening price of the gold market is 120 yuan. (5th Dispatch)

(Wuhu) The financial circles of Wuhu held a meeting on the 5th regarding the currency law, and unanimously approved it. They also elected representatives to meet with the authorities to request that they maintain the market and stabilize prices. The money market has not been affected. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Anqing) The Provincial Government issued a proclamation on the 5th to strictly enforce the currency policy, strictly prohibiting rumors, and summoned the responsible persons of various banks and chambers of commerce in Anhui to give instructions on everything. The Anhui branch of the Central Bank of China has set up a legal tender exchange office and will establish an exchange office for mixed silver materials within this month. (5th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) He Chengjun received a telegram from the Hankou Pacification Headquarters on the 5th, saying that the Hankou Municipal Government received an order from the Ministry of Finance on the night of the 3rd, and immediately convened the banking and business circles to discuss everything. A public notice was immediately distributed. The market was stable on the 4th. The prices of both imported and exported goods in foreign trade did not rise. The prices of daily necessities in the city, such as rice and charcoal, did not change, etc. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to the Rice Industry Association, since the change in currency policy, the price of rice in the capital has increased due to the sharp rise in the price of rice in Shanghai and Wuhu. In the past two days, the price has risen by four or five dimes per stone. In the past two days, the arrival of rice from Anhui and local gangs has been smooth. The price of cooked rice from Anhui is below 8.2 yuan per stone. The three types of cooked rice produced in Jiangning, Lishui, and Jurong, "Yang cooked," "top cooked," and "black cooked," are all 9 yuan per stone. The price of Su Geng rice from Wuxi is about 10.5 yuan per stone. The selling price of rice shops and stores must also add 6 dimes per stone for living expenses, i.e., Yang cooked rice sells for 9.6 yuan, and Anhui Xian cooked rice sells for 8.8 yuan. It is speculated that there is still a trend of continued price increases. (5th Dispatch)

(Changsha) After the central government's order to unify the issuance and centralize reserves arrived on the 5th, all banks and money houses uniformly complied, and the market was stable. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Changsha) Because the silver and money industry received the order later, it implemented cash centralization starting on the 5th, and the market was stable. (5th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) After a meeting between the money industry exchange clearing house and various banks, it was announced that legal tender would be the standard, and banknotes and cash would be on par. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce will hold a meeting today to discuss the promotion of legal tender and will advise various industries to suppress and stabilize prices. (5th Dispatch)

(Jinan) After the currency reform order was issued, the financial situation in this city was stable. The Bankers Association held a meeting and resolved to work together to implement it: 1. The industry will implement flat exchange rates and settle accounts in Shanghai. 2. No remittance fees will be charged for remittances to stores, only a small amount of postage and handling fees will be charged. 3. The allocation of funds in this city will be strictly restricted, and banks will no longer accept them. All inflows and outflows will be made in legal tender and banknotes approved by the government. Telegraphic transfers have risen from 15 yuan to 1 yuan. However, there is general concern that food prices will rise, and people are now competing to buy and store wheat, with over 1,400 tons traded. The silver and money industries will hold a meeting at the Bankers Association on the 6th. (5th Dispatch)

(Chongqing) Xi Yan, the manager of the Chongqing branch of the Central Bank of China, convened a meeting of the responsible persons of the city's silver and money industries at 2 p.m. on the 5th to explain in detail the emergency decrees announced by the Ministry of Finance on the 3rd. All banks and money houses were able to deeply understand the spirit of this currency reform and unanimously expressed their firm support. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) After the Ministry of Finance issued the new legal tender order, the three banks in Bing City, the Provincial Bank, the Reclamation Bank, and the Railway Salt Bank, etc., before receiving a formal order from the Provincial Government, each bank continued to redeem cash as before. Although the number of redeemers was higher than in the past, the banks were able to cope with them due to sufficient reserves. In addition, the transactions of various firms in the market were still quite calm. The Provincial Bank and the Money Industry Association are now holding meetings to discuss countermeasures and have decided to temporarily maintain the status quo of the common use of banknotes and cash. The Bank of China, etc., has received an order from the head office. (4th Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) After the Ministry of Finance's unified currency law was issued here, the financial situation in the market turned stable. The authorities today summoned the banking community to show the main points of maintaining finance and telegraphed a report to the Beijing newspaper. (5th Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Xiamen branches of banks such as the Xiamen Central, South, Industrial, etc., received telegrams from the Shanghai head office yesterday to check the amount of banknotes issued so as to report them separately, and to continue to use them as usual. No new notes will be issued in the future. The banks have already issued banknotes, including two million from Xiamen Central, 1.3 million from South, 1.5 million from Industrial, and 1.4 million from Farmers. The Xiamen branch of the Provincial Bank will be established in December and will issue corner notes. The financial situation in this city is still stable yesterday and today. However, the price of small foreign currency has soared, with one foreign currency yuan only exchanging for 11.7 dimes. In addition, the Hong Kong government will also implement a currency system prohibiting the export of silver. The premium for Hong Kong currency, which was previously 480 yuan per 1,000 yuan, has fallen to 240 yuan yesterday. It is expected that it will be equal to the national currency in the future. (5th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) A certain banker said that after the central government announced that silver was nationalized, it was beneficial to Guangdong currency. Currently, the Guangdong province's national tax revenue is still calculated in small foreign currency. On the 5th, Hong Kong paper and silver dollars fell in price, and the paper currency of the three banks, the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, rose slightly. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong Silver Industry Association held a meeting on the evening of the 4th to discuss the central government's control of the currency system. Because Guangdong has always used the small foreign currency system, the market is not affected, and there is no need to discuss countermeasures for the time being. (5th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Shantou and Haikou in Guangdong have always used silver dollars as the standard and have decided to comply with the new currency law controlled by the Ministry of Finance. As for Guangzhou and other parts of Guangdong, which have always used small foreign currency as the standard, how to handle it will be decided after detailed consultation with the authorities. (5th Dispatch)

Educational Broadcasting Special Issue Wang Jie Inscription

Youth and the Nation (Part 1) 42

(Lectures given to middle school students nationwide on October 29th and 31st)

Qian Duansheng, Professor at National Central University

"Youth are the future masters of the nation." This saying is not only commonly used in China, a country that respects scholars, as a way to encourage young people who are engrossed in their studies, but also in other countries, youth are similarly praised. In the 19th century, Italy had a very famous patriot named Mazzini. He was the founder of the Young Italy movement, the greatest contributor to the unification of Italy, and also a model youth of both ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. He was one of Italy's three heroes, and also the most outstanding of the two heroes. I remember him saying something like this when he was arousing Italian youth scattered in various European countries.

If youth are the future masters of any country, then youth are especially the future masters of China. The general population of China has not received education, while youth are currently receiving modern education. At this critical juncture when the nation is facing dire difficulties, youth with higher intelligence naturally bear a greater responsibility for the country. In order to prepare for bearing the responsibilities they should bear in the future, youth should first understand the nation, and second, strive to be good citizens.

(1) To Understand Our Nation

Youth should naturally have a strong sense of patriotism for the nation. The reason why China's national strength is not as good as other major countries in the world certainly has various different reasons, but the weakness of the people's patriotism can be said to be the biggest and most fundamental reason. Why is the patriotism of our people so weak? Because the people's concept of the nation is too weak. The majority of the people have not received education, they do not know what the nation is, so they naturally have no feelings for the nation. Therefore, to love the country, one must first know everything about the country.

Political scientists believe that a nation is composed of three elements: people, land, and sovereignty. People and land are material elements, and sovereignty can be said to be a spiritual element.

People are the population. A country must have a population; without a population, there cannot be a country. This is self-evident.

But a country cannot be established with only a population and no land. At the same time, this so-called land must be fixed. Ancient nomadic peoples could not establish a country because they did not have fixed land. Without fixed land, there cannot be a government, and without a government, sovereignty cannot be maintained.

So what is sovereignty? Sovereignty, also known as the right to rule, is the right of the people to handle all public affairs within the national territory. To manage public affairs within the national territory, the people must establish a government. If the people's right to rule is complete, then this government is certainly supreme, and no other people except the citizens of the country can interfere. If the people's right to rule is not complete, for example, if country A (let's call it country A) cannot independently control its diplomatic power and must obtain the consent of country B, then the government of country A is not an independent government, the people of country A do not have complete management rights, which is not complete sovereignty, and country A does not become a nation.

The reason why a country cannot survive without sovereignty is very simple. A province has the people of the province, the land of the province, and the government of the province. A city also has the people of the city, the land of the city, and the government of the city. The difference between a nation and a province or city is that the power of the national government is supreme, while the provincial and municipal governments must be under the jurisdiction of the central government. In other words, a nation is independent, while provinces and cities are not independent; independent entities have sovereignty, while non-independent entities do not have sovereignty. If a group of people, with land and a government, or a place with people and a government, is considered to have established a nation, then wouldn't a province or a city also establish a nation? Wouldn't even a village be considered a nation? That is certainly incorrect. Therefore, political scientists insist on sovereignty as one of the three elements of a nation; merely having the two material elements of people and land cannot form a nation; it must also have sovereignty to become a nation.

Our China is an independent country, and of course, our China also has the three elements of people, land, and sovereignty. So what about our people, land, and sovereignty? These are the matters that youth should be most familiar with. To be familiar with these matters, one must know the strengths and weaknesses of these three aspects in order to truly love the country. Knowing only the strengths and not the weaknesses can easily lead to a kind of vanity, and knowing only the weaknesses and not the strengths can easily lead to discouragement, or even make one feel that our country is not lovable.

Let's first talk about the people of China. The people of China have many advantages, but also many weaknesses. The first advantage is that our country is almost a nation-state. Nation is different from citizen. Citizens are the people of a country, while a nation is a combination of people, based on bloodline, language, religion, customs, habits, and history. The bloodline, language, etc., of the people of a country can be completely different, but the bloodline, language, etc., of members of the same nation must be largely the same. A nation-state is a country whose people belong to the same nation. The so-called nationalism in modern times is the movement of a nation seeking independence and becoming a country. A non-nation-state is a country whose people do not belong to the same nation. The Netherlands is a nation-state because its people all belong to the Dutch nation, and their bloodline, language, religion, customs, habits, and history are all the same. Belgium is not a nation-state because the people of Belgium belong to two nations: in the south are the Walloons, who are close to the French nation, and in the north are the Flemish, who are close to the Dutch nation. A nation-state is superior to a non-nation-state because the unity of a nation-state is stronger. Although it is said that the people of our China have five ethnic groups—Han, Manchu, Mongol, Hui, and Tibetan—the Chinese nation actually accounts for more than 98 percent of the 400 million people. The Manchus have long merged with the Han people into the Chinese nation. The Hui people and the Han people are very close in everything except religion. Only the Mongols, Tibetans, and some small ethnic groups in Xinjiang, as well as the uncivilized Miao people in the southwest, cannot be considered to be of the same nation as the Han people. However, these people have also had a common political history with the Han people for six or seven hundred years, so they are very close to the Han people. A country with so many people, and so many people almost united under the same nation, is something that no other country in the world can match, and it is also something that we can be most proud of. The Soviet Union is considered the largest country in the world, with a population second only to China and India, but only 120 million of the Soviet Union's 160 million people belong to the Great Russian nation, and the rest are different nations. The Soviet Union still cannot match China, and the other countries are even further behind.

Regarding the people, the second advantage of our country is that the Chinese nation is not only the largest but also a nation with the longest history and the oldest culture. From this long history, we can understand the spirit of struggle of our ancestors, and we can discover the great contributions of our nation to humanity. The Chinese nation has never been a nation that was born in comfort and grew up in comfort, nor has it been a nation without virtue or ability. In the process of our nation's development, we have experienced countless foreign invasions. From the Yi and Di of the Three Dynasties, through the Xiongnu of the Qin and Han dynasties, the Turks and Uyghurs of the Tang dynasty, the Liao and Jin dynasties of the Song dynasty, the Mongols, and up to the Manchus of the Ming dynasty, our Chinese nation was almost in danger of extinction at all times. However, because of the thick quality of the nation, these invading nations were either destroyed by us or assimilated by us, and in the end, it was still the victory of the Chinese nation. Since the eastward invasion of European powers in the last century, our country has again been in danger of being reduced to a colony at all times, and in recent years, the life of the country has been hanging by a thread. At this extremely urgent beginning, we should have a stronger national self-confidence. I believe that the more familiar we are with the past history of our nation, the more we will be able to increase our confidence in our nation.

But our people also have three major shortcomings. The first shortcoming is the underdevelopment of the people's knowledge. In civilized countries of the world, the people who are illiterate will never exceed 30 percent. However, at least 80 percent of our people are illiterate and have not received education. Because they are illiterate and have not received education, they cannot know themselves, nor can they know others. The wealth and power of others, the Chinese people do not know, the invasion of others, the Chinese people do not understand; at the same time, the glorious history of the Chinese nation, the Chinese people do not know to cherish. Therefore, although the Chinese people are of the same nation, the national consciousness and the concept of the nation are very weak, and this shortcoming has become a fatal wound for our country.

Second, our Chinese nation lacks a scientific mind. Because of the lack of a scientific mind, although our previous culture has its immortal aspects, it does not even have the ability to follow in the footsteps of modern industrial culture. Japan's ancient culture is very close to our ancient culture; but Japan's material civilization is no less than that of Western countries. Why? Because the Japanese have a scientific mind. Our scientific minds are inferior to others, so industrial culture has not yet developed, but in today's world, without industrial culture, one cannot establish a nation. Therefore, for the sake of our nation, anything that hinders the development of a scientific mind, such as the ancient imperial examination education, must be strictly prohibited, while education that is close to nature must be vigorously promoted. (To be continued)

Wang River Dike Restoration and Breach Closing Project to be Completed by Deadline, Central Government Bears Expenses of 10 Million Yuan 43

(Nanjing) The Economic Commission, in order to determine the funds for this year's river dike restoration and breach closing, previously ordered the Yellow River and Yangtze River Commissions to jointly conduct surveys with relevant agencies, and set a deadline of the 20th of last month to submit reports for review. It is now known that after receiving and reviewing the reports, the central government will be responsible for the expenses of the main dikes, while local governments will be responsible for raising funds for the people's dikes. The central government will bear approximately 10 million yuan. The Executive Yuan has approved a letter instructing the Ministry of Finance to allocate funds and forward them to the provincial governments to begin construction immediately, with a deadline of completion before the next flood season. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 5th)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Sends Personnel to Inspect Donghai Dike Project 44

(Xuzhou) The Lintou Dike in Donghai, which was built to prevent the Yellow River, is more than eighty li long and has now been completed. The provincial government has dispatched Chen Jintang to Donghai for inspection. The dike is six chi high, twelve chi wide at the top, and entirely constructed with wooden piles, making the project very solid. Furthermore, the anti-Yellow River dike from Xinpu to Longju, which was previously breached by floodwaters, has also been reinforced and rebuilt. A watchtower is built every li, and the project is scheduled to be completed within five days. The water level in Donghai has already dropped by about two Chinese feet. If it does not continue to rise, it is hoped that wheat can be planted in the low-lying fields. (Special dispatch from the 5th)

(Xuzhou) According to a report from Donghai, the riverbed of Qingkou River in Ganyu is silted up, and mountain floods often cause disasters. Approval has now been obtained from the provincial government to thoroughly dredge the river this winter and begin construction within days, with completion scheduled for this year. (Special dispatch from the 5th)

Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce and Banking Industry Hold Joint Meeting 58

—Supporting the Policy of Currency System Reform—

According to reports from Hangzhou, the Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, in order to stabilize public sentiment in response to the government's implementation of the new currency policy, convened an emergency temporary meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 5th. Representatives from the Municipal Government, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, and the Commercial Affairs Administration also participated. The meeting, chaired by Cheng Zhenji, resolved: (1) to issue a public notice to advise merchants and the public to earnestly abide by the laws and regulations and not to raise prices under any pretext; (2) to compile a notice and request the Public Security Bureau to distribute it to citizens; (3) to schedule a joint meeting of various trade associations at 3:00 p.m. on November 6; (4) to send a letter to the banking and money industries requesting them to earnestly discuss ways to raise funds and revitalize the market; (5) to telegraph the Ministry of Finance in support of the new policy of currency system reform, requesting the implementation of real estate mortgage measures to ensure early implementation, further consolidate the effectiveness of the currency system, relieve the market, and revive the countryside. At 11:00 a.m., the banking and money industries held a joint meeting at the Central Bank, attended by more than 60 people. The meeting resolved: (1) that the exact amount of cash reserves in each bank and money shop as of today should be reported to the Central Bank that evening and compiled into a report to the Shanghai Central Bank Headquarters; (2) that each bank and money shop should set up a cash exchange for exchanging legal tender as an agency for exchanging legal tender. The Zhejiang Provincial Government decided at its routine meeting today that counties in remote areas where it is impossible to exchange legal tender should be allowed to handle the matter at their discretion. As for the one-yuan legal tender bills of the three banks, because they are used to replace silver dollars, the demand for them has suddenly increased. A telegram has been sent to Shanghai requesting that they be shipped to Hangzhou in batches, totaling about one million yuan, which will be circulated in the market and will be sufficient to meet the demand. Furthermore, the financial and money markets on the 5th were still volatile compared to the 4th. Each legal tender yuan was worth 12 jiao and 10 wen in silver, and copper coins recovered to 3,450 wen. The gold market has opened, and both Ye Chi gold are priced at 120 yuan. (November 5th)

Suzhou - A Unique Case of Filicide

Wu Chucheng, a partner in the Ziyang Temple on Fourth Avenue in Shanghai, and his wife, Ms. Jiang, lived with their thirteen-year-old son, Wu Zaowang, at 14 1/2 Guimen Street, outside the Lumen Gate in Suzhou. They opened the Wu Yongcheng Oil and Wine Shop. However, Ms. Wu Jiang had an affair with a fellow villager, Wang Shiqing (Jixiang). Because her son discovered this and spread it around, it aroused her shame and anger. On the evening of the 4th, Wu Zaowang returned home from school and was strangled to death by his mother with a rope. She then pretended that he had committed suicide and reported it to the police station through a neighbor. Ms. Wu Jiang (also known as Guiyuan) was taken to the police station, and the District Procuratorate was notified. At 3:00 p.m. on the 5th, the District Procuratorate sent personnel to examine the body to verify the case. Also, Yang Shungen, a farmer from Chuanjinggang, Yanmu Pavilion, in the rural area of Suzhou, returned home from outside at noon the day before yesterday. For some unknown reason, he suddenly held a kitchen knife and hacked his three-year-old son to death. His eight-year-old son was also hacked on the head, but the injury was minor and he is currently being treated. The responsible police station has reported the case to the District Court and requested personnel to conduct an examination.

Wuxi

Organizing an Air Defense Committee

The county government believes that air defense is a necessary common sense for the people. Therefore, it has scheduled regular air defense exercises. Yesterday (the 5th) at 3:00 p.m., it convened representatives from the party, government, military, and various agencies, organizations, and schools to hold a preparatory meeting for air defense exercises. It was decided to organize an air defense committee, which would be divided into six groups: general affairs, publicity, intelligence, management, alarm, and suppression. The responsible personnel for each group were immediately appointed to begin work. It is expected that personnel will be dispatched within days to inspect and control lighting equipment.

Implementing National Labor Service

The Jiangsu Provincial National Labor Service Regulations stipulate that the period from November 1 of this year to March 31 of next year is the water conservancy service season. During this period, all able-bodied men between the ages of 18 and 50, regardless of whether they are civil servants or students, must perform labor service. The focus of this labor service is to dredge rivers and ponds. Each able-bodied man must serve for at least three days. After receiving the order, the Wuxi County Government immediately submitted it to the 63rd District Heads' Meeting and decided that each district should conduct a detailed investigation of the rivers and ponds to be dredged in accordance with the provincial regulations and report them by the 10th of this month. The Construction Bureau will then dispatch technical personnel to conduct surveys in each district. The minimum standard for each district is to dredge 50,000 cubic meters of rivers and ponds. It will supervise and urge each district to use the Baojia system to mobilize able-bodied men. This initiative will not only cultivate the people's labor habits but also provide considerable assistance to the future of national construction. As for the labor service methods for civil servants, students, and soldiers, the county government is currently drafting them in detail.

Market Chaos After Cash is Discontinued

After the Ministry of Finance stipulated on the 4th that banknotes from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications would be legal tender and that cash could not be used, the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, Central China Bank, Continental Bank, Siming Bank, Industrial Bank, Xingye Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Communications Bank, and Farmers Bank in this city yesterday sealed up all the silver and silver dollars they had on hand and awaited instructions from the head office. The silver firms in this city also made long-distance calls to the silver firms in Shanghai yesterday to inquire. It was reported that the Shanghai gold and silver markets were still operating as usual, but the price of gold remained firm and tended to rise. As for future developments, it is necessary to wait for the Shanghai silver firms to hold a meeting to discuss the matter and ask the authorities for instructions before making a decision. In general, it has no fundamental impact on those who specialize in selling utensils. The price of gold in the market in this city has risen to 117 yuan per tael. The rice market has also seen a sharp rise of seven or eight jiao. Yesterday, the market suddenly fell by three or four jiao. New white japonica rice was 10.2 jiao per dan, down to 9.78 jiao. Japonica rice was 5.05 yuan. There are three reasons for the sudden rise and fall: (1) various banks purchased goods and stockpiled them; (2) some silk cocoon merchants purchased a large amount of rice with the profits from silk cocoons and stockpiled it to wait for a good price to sell; (3) the rice industry believes that the Ministry of Finance has issued emergency regulations to reform the currency system, and various banks can lend as much as possible, paying the funds to merchants without relying on the income of buyers, and using the loans from the banks to purchase rice and other grains. However, various banks still restrict lending, so the rice market suddenly fell. Pawnshops have been very busy recently. According to people in the pawn industry yesterday, the price of gold has soared recently, and many customers have come to redeem gold items. It is estimated that after redeeming them, they are exchanging them for cash at various silver firms. In addition, the prices of goods in various industries have been relatively stable due to the sharp drop in the price of foreign currency. However, yesterday the price of foreign currency fell from 2,990 wen to 2,690 wen, causing market chaos and public panic.

Changzhou

Chamber of Commerce Auxiliary Coin Balance Meeting

The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce Auxiliary Coin Balance Market Price Committee held a meeting on the afternoon of the 4th, chaired by Yu Yicheng, to discuss the following matters: (1) The market price of jiaozi and copper coins in neighboring counties such as Shenxi has already risen sharply. Should the market price in this county also rise accordingly to achieve balance? The public decided that the market price would be as follows: copper coins 3,050 wen, jiaozi 12 jiao and 5 fen, jiaozi blanks 2,440 wen, and small foreign currency 82% of the Shanghai large foreign currency. (2) The market price of jiaozi and copper coins in neighboring counties is bound to fluctuate in the future. Should this committee hold meetings every day? It was decided that the committee would hold meetings for one week from today to the 11th to stabilize the market. The meeting time was set at 4:00 p.m., and all committee members were required to attend the meeting on time.

Ningbo

A Large Number of Fishing Boats are Stolen and Kidnapped

Although the fishing season in Dinghai Shenjiamen this year is better than in previous years, many fishermen are unable to go fishing because they are trapped by the cost of fishing. Therefore, less than one-third of the large fishing fleets went to sea this year compared to last year. In addition, the low prices hurt the fishing industry, causing the fishing village economy to plummet. Recently, the fishing area has been near Langgang Ocean. On the evening of the 31st, a large number of pirates suddenly appeared in the Guanshan Ocean area and seized more than 20 fishing boats belonging to Zhang Da Niang, Jiang A Xiao, Xia Dingxing, Xin Yunqing, and others. The pirate leaders, Jin Shunan and Huang Chunshan, sent letters to the families of the seized fishermen, instructing them to prepare funds and go to a designated location to redeem their relatives. The other fishing boats that were not kidnapped returned to Shenjiamen to report the incident. At that time, the fishing industry association and other fishing industry organizations had no warships to dispatch and could not pursue the pirates. The next afternoon, various fishing industry organizations held a meeting at the Fish Warehouse Guild to discuss the matter. It was learned that no ships had been seen patrolling the ocean recently, which is a major threat to the safety of fishermen. It was decided to send telegrams to the Security Office, the Fishing Industry Police Bureau, the Water Police Bureau, and other agencies, requesting them to quickly send warships to patrol and protect the ocean. At the same time, a telegram was sent to the county government requesting them to appeal on behalf of the fishermen to ensure the safety of the fishing industry.

A Double Life 59

— Feng Zikai

Western culture has invaded China with an irresistible force. At the same time, Chinese culture has stubbornly preserved its traditions. As a result, in the thoughts and lives of Chinese people, a state of coexistence of new and old cultures appears everywhere. This is called a double life. For example, here a small family is being organized, and there, the practice of nine generations living together is being encouraged. Here, divorce advertisements are being published, and there, chastity arches are being built. Even these two states appear in the same family or in the same person, creating all kinds of worries and pains.

Everyone only knows to blame the instability of people's livelihoods over the years on major causes such as natural disasters, man-made calamities, internal strife, and foreign aggression. Little do they know that, apart from these, there is another cause that most directly makes people's livelihoods unstable, which is this double life. It can make the general public look left and right, look around, and be at a loss as to what to do, constantly wandering on the wrong path in life. It can enable all kinds of words and deeds to find a basis for establishment, and all kinds of evils to find a reason for defense, so that right and wrong are reversed, and black and white are confused. How many tens of millions of people in recent China have been full of hesitation and painstaking efforts for the sake of the direction of life, and finally fell into blind obedience and suffered failure! To say nothing else, just looking at the smallest thing in the double life—the coexistence of the lunar and solar calendars—is enough to cause people a lot of trouble!

"Sincerity within will surely manifest itself externally," is it only true of individuals? Society is also like this. In our country's folk society, which is living a double life, incompatible states of temporal errors are revealed everywhere, forming a wonderful world of cartoons. Cartoons have become quite popular in our country recently, and the double life is the main reason for this. Try taking a leisurely walk in the city streets and observing the current situation quietly, and you will surely discover various incompatible states of double life, which are laughable or alarming. A streamlined car is sometimes seen next to a sedan chair being carried. In front of a tram, there are sometimes two "Silence" signs being carried on shoulders. A pair of wooden clogs is walking on a cement sidewalk. Six red gauze lanterns are hanging near neon lights. A stone arch bridge is lined up next to a railway. An ancient temple is sandwiched between two high-rise buildings. ... Walking into a house; sometimes you will see "Heaven Bestows Blessings" hanging in the drawing room of a Western-style house, with incense burners, candle holders, and two strings of paper gold ingots placed for worship. On the door opposite the flush toilet, there is a yellow paper strip that says, "Jiang Taigong is here, nothing is taboo." If it is winter, you will see people wearing top hats sitting on Ning-style beds; people with bronze braziers in their hands holding water pipes. If it is a festive day, you will see ancient brides and modern grooms, and people wearing costumes performing kneeling ceremonies. If it is for a patient, you can even see Western doctors and Taoist priests walking into the same family. ...

But this is not a state unique to China. Japan is also like this. Formally, and also in terms of art, Japan can be said to be the country with the most flourishing Eastern style. Various styles of ancient Eastern life, such as sitting on the floor, walking in wooden clogs, and men's and women's clothing, etiquette, etc., have long been abandoned in China, but are still practiced in Japan today. When the Meiji Restoration occurred and Western culture was introduced to Japan, the state of double life in their society was probably even more laughable and alarming than what we have now. Ukiyo-e master Yoshitoshi's works include paintings satirizing the incompatible state at that time. He depicted members of the Diet in the early Meiji era wearing "haori" (Japanese outer jacket), with a "hakama" (waist apron), while wearing Western top hats and leather shoes, creating a comical appearance. Modern Japanese art theorists also curse the double life in Tokyo. For example: wearing wooden clogs and riding a tram, an old-fashioned bride and a groom in a tuxedo, a Western-style building and a Japanese-style old house, torii (wooden archways) lined up, and people in Western clothes kneeling down to perform Japanese etiquette when they meet… They say that the coexistence of these Western and Eastern styles makes the street scene incompatible and the environment ugly, which is "non-artistic." They are striving to demand improvement, harmony, and the artisticization of the city streets. Artists, art lovers, and those who care about "city appearance" living in the current Chinese society probably all have the same feeling about their curses and demands?

This kind of cursing and demanding has its own legitimate reasons, but that incompatible appearance is also an inevitable product. Western culture has rushed into the East with an irresistible force, and it is impossible not to accept it.

However, who can sweep away all Eastern old habits and make it completely Westernized immediately? Judging from the hearts of artists, it seems that they hope to be completely Westernized immediately, so that people standing on the streets of Tokyo or Shanghai feel as if they are standing on the streets of Paris or London. Otherwise, they would simply want to be completely Eastern-style, so that people living in modern society feel as if they are living in ancient society. However, both are impossible. It is certainly impossible to return to ancient times; how easy is it to completely Westernize? Even if it is "easy," (Note: I remember a certain ancient person said that the word "easy" is not connected, but rather the two words "how" and "allow" are connected, now I force it.) our noses are not naturally high, our eyes are not naturally blue, and our skin is not naturally white, so this Westernization is also incomplete, then what attitude should we take towards this matter when we are born in modern China? Are we going to always live this laughable and incompatible double life?

No, our future has its own new road waiting to be opened up. This is the road of "chemical combination" of Eastern and Western cultures, and it can also be said to be the road of "great harmony" of world cultures. Material civilization originated in the West, but it is not exclusive to the West, and should be a gift of "the times" that all ethnic groups in the present world must accept. Most of the various material civilization constructions we have in our country today are transported hard from the West and inserted raw and ruthlessly into our country. All the laughable and incompatible double lives are produced from this. In other words, in our current life, Eastern and Western cultures are "mixed" together, so there is a double life. We must teach them to "combine chemically" to produce a third kind of new life, and then can we get rid of the various ugliness and pains mentioned above. Furthermore, the West will not always be an advanced nation. In the future world, there will definitely be mutual influence and mutual assimilation, and gradually move towards the road of "great harmony."

We should not hesitate to abandon various old habits, and we should not be afraid to accept various new trends. As long as we take "reasonableness" as the basis and strive to create a new life, we will be in line with the purpose of world harmony. It is said that the Japanese once had a proposal to abolish their original script and use Roman characters arranged horizontally. There is also an attempt to abolish the separation of "Japanese painting department" and "Western painting department" in art schools and only set up a "painting department." However, it has not yet succeeded. I remember that a few people in China also tried to use horizontally written, phonetic alphabet-spelled national sounds, but no one paid attention. This is certainly not easy to do. But I am foolishly dreaming here: setting up armaments and engaging in wars is nothing more than seeking the happiness of human life. If all countries in the world could save all the expenses used for armaments and wars and transfer them to the construction costs of the future "world of great harmony", it would certainly not be difficult to achieve, and the lives of all mankind would certainly be much happier! The world's artists will surely rejoice even more! Unfortunately, this is just my dream.
