Education News

Experimental Methods for Short-Term Primary School System 113

On the 4th, the Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education bureaus of each province and city, stating, "Upon reviewing the implementation of compulsory education, each locality should establish a one-year short-term primary school during the first phase and a two-year short-term primary school during the second phase. In order to improve the various management methods of these short-term primary schools and facilitate implementation, the Experimental Methods for the Short-Term Primary School System have been established. According to the regulations of these methods, affiliated primary schools or experimental primary schools of domestic normal universities, university education colleges, independent education colleges, provincial and municipal normal schools, and other primary schools with experimental capabilities should conduct experiments in accordance with designated experimental matters. It is hereby ordered that these methods be inspected, sent, and forwarded to your subordinates for compliance and reporting." This order.

Experimental Methods for the Short-Term Primary School System

(1) In order to improve the various management methods of short-term primary schools and facilitate implementation, affiliated primary schools or experimental primary schools of domestic normal universities, university education colleges, independent education colleges, provincial and municipal normal schools, and other primary schools with experimental capabilities should conduct experiments. Each of the aforementioned short-term primary school experimental classes should have at least one class per school.

(2) Experimental matters are as follows: (1) Experimentation and revision of the Ministry's promulgated Interim Curriculum Standards and Textbooks for One-Year Short-Term Primary Schools; (2) Experimental compilation and editing of ideal Curriculum Standards and Textbooks for One-Year Short-Term Primary Schools; (3) Teaching methods for Short-Term Primary Schools; (4) Experimentation with Curriculum, Textbooks, and Teaching Methods for Two-Year Short-Term Primary Schools, with the addition of the two-part ordinary primary school system, etc.

(3) Items 2 and 4 of the preceding article shall be experimented on by the affiliated primary schools or experimental schools of normal universities, university education colleges, or independent education colleges. Items 1 and 3 of the preceding article, and the added items, shall be experimented on by the affiliated primary schools or provincial experimental primary schools of provincial and municipal normal schools. However, provincial and municipal normal school affiliated primary schools or provincial experimental primary schools that wish to experiment on Items 2 and 4 of the preceding article may request approval from the competent education authority to forward it to the Ministry of Education for implementation. The same applies to affiliated primary schools or experimental schools of normal universities, university education colleges, and independent education colleges that wish to simultaneously experiment on Items 1 and 3.

(4) Those experimenting with Items 2 and 4 of Article 2 must submit a plan to the Ministry of Education for approval before proceeding.

(5) Other education authorities that wish to conduct experiments on Items 1 and 3 of Article 2 and the added items must submit a plan and request approval from the provincial and municipal compulsory education committees before proceeding.

(6) Experimenters must submit a first report to the competent education authority before the summer vacation of 1936 and forward it to the Ministry of Education.

(7) Those with excellent experimental results may be appropriately rewarded by the Ministry of Education.

Little Boy (86) 123

— Original by Ms. Alcott of America, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

One evening, a cool breeze was blowing, and the children were all asleep except for the older ones who were still bathing by the creek. Mrs. Pei was in the sitting room undressing Tandy when suddenly he shouted, "Ah, my Donald!" pointing to the moonlit window.

"No, darling, he's not there; that's just the beautiful moon," his mother said.

"No, no, Donald is at a window; Tandy saw him," the little boy insisted, looking very excited.

"That may be possible," Mrs. Pei said, rushing to the window, hoping to confirm the child's words. But there was no face, and not a trace of anyone could be found. She called his name, took Tandy, who was only wearing a small undershirt, to the front door, and had him call out too, thinking that the little boy's voice might be louder than hers. But there was no answer, and nothing could be found. So, they returned dejectedly. However, Tandy didn't think it was just the moon, so after he was already asleep in his little bed, he would still look up from time to time and ask, "Is Donald 'coming back soon'?"

Soon he fell asleep, the children all went to bed, and the house gradually became quiet, only occasionally broken by the chirping of crickets disturbing the peaceful night. Mrs. Pei sat doing sewing work, because the large basket was always full of socks with holes big enough to swallow an elephant. At the same time, she was thinking about the lost child. She decided that the little boy was wrong, so she didn't go to tell Mr. Pei, lest the child's fantasy interrupt his work. After all, when did that poor man ever have any time to himself except after the children were in bed? He was busy writing letters. It was already after ten o'clock when she stood up to close the door of the house. She couldn't help but linger a moment on the steps, admiring the lovely scene. Suddenly, she noticed something white on one of the many haystacks scattered on the lawn, something she didn't recognize. The children had been playing there all afternoon, and Mrs. Pei assumed it was just Nan's discarded white hat, so she went to retrieve it. But as she approached, she saw that it was not a hat or a handkerchief, but just a shirt sleeve, with a yellowed hand sticking out. She ran over to the haystack, and there slept Don, sleeping soundly.

Yesterday's Basketball Friendly Match: Hujiang Fought Hard Against Guanghua 127

Hujiang Won 26-24

The Outcome Was Determined in Overtime; Guanghua Lost by One Point

Guanghua and Hujiang Middle Schools held a basketball friendly match at the Guanghua gymnasium yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. The referee was Lu Xiangqian. In the first half, Hujiang took a commanding lead with 17-4. Unexpectedly, at the start of the second half, Guanghua's new forces entered the field, making a rapid comeback. By the end of regulation time, the score was tied at 22-22. After both sides agreed to extend the game by five minutes, Hujiang finally secured the final victory by two points. The game was full of twists and turns, and the atmosphere was tense. A reporter from Guoguang News Agency has the following report:

In the First Half, Hujiang Took the Lead

Just after 3:00 PM, the match began. Hujiang's left forward, Chen Weiquan, went straight up the side, making a short pass. Center Tang Baojia caught it perfectly, and with a wave of his hand, hit the target. In less than a minute, Tang Baojia scored again, and Hu Qipeng added to the momentum with another point. Hujiang had already scored six points, while Guanghua had achieved nothing. They had no choice but to call a timeout and bring in substitute players. However, Hujiang's momentum was strong, and a mere cup of water could not save a burning cart of firewood. Guanghua's new player, Ouyang Ming, didn't make any contributions after being brought in, and was instead penalized for a foul, losing a point. Hujiang pressed forward relentlessly, taking a huge lead with a score of 17-0. At that time, there were only about three minutes left in the first half. Guanghua quickly brought in Chao Jianzhang to take on the important role of center. Sure enough, he scored a direct hit, breaking the duck egg. Zhang Fuyuan disregarded his own safety and made another miraculous contribution, ending the first half with a score of 17-4 in Hujiang's overwhelming victory.

Guanghua Worked Hard and Tied the Score

The second half began, and Hujiang's Sa Fengquan and Lu Zhongyu retired after their accomplishments. Guanghua suddenly became enlightened, and their passing and shooting became effortless. Zhang Dangyuan and Zhang Yaoqin stepped up without hesitation, scoring six points in a row. Hujiang only had the new player Kang Guogan score a point from a free throw, and Tang Baojia score two points from a long shot. After that, it was all about Guanghua. Ye Wensheng, Gu Liangren, Zhang Fuyuan, and others rode and galloped together, all making contributions, adding another eight points. At this time, the score was extremely close, with only a two-point difference. The atmosphere in the stands was tense to the extreme. Hujiang's general Tang Baojia had been tightly marked by Guanghua, and the hero had no place to show his skills. Fortunately, left forward Chen Weiquan suddenly emerged as a surprise force, making a contribution and returning. Guanghua's Xie Zongming and Ye Wensheng, seeing the imminent danger, scored two goals in a row, restoring Guanghua. The regulation time had arrived, with Guanghua at 18 and Hujiang at five. The overall result was a tie at 22-22.

In Overtime, Hujiang Declared Victory

The game was extended by five minutes. At this time, both sides went back and forth, refusing to give in. Guanghua, seeing that the crisis had passed, was unwilling to lose the city again. Hujiang was careful and cautious. Three minutes passed, and neither side scored. Guanghua's right guard, Ye Wensheng, roared loudly and actually scored, causing a burst of cheers like firecrackers. However, Guanghua's joy was short-lived. In a moment of carelessness, Hujiang's Tang Baojia broke free from his shackles and tied the score again. There were still three seconds left. Guanghua was full of hope that nothing would happen, but unexpectedly, Sa Fengquan approached the city and with a wave of his hand, the ball fell into the net. The whistle blew, ending the game. The ball happened to go into the basket. The overall result was 26-24, with Hujiang winning. Yesterday's performance of both sides is as follows:

Money Market Sees Relief 136

Subsidiary Coins Lack Public Exchange Rate, Prices Remain Inconsistent

Since the government stipulated the legal tender (fabi) a few days ago, the money market initially did not know how to adapt. After Chief Financial Officer Kong Xiangxi provided a detailed explanation, the market sentiment has gradually eased. Therefore, the exchange rate for foreign currency drafts in the morning and afternoon markets showed a marked relaxation, decreasing by two cents compared to the previous day, calculated at eighteen cents. The head commission ("hua tou," or "slippage fee") plus water ("jia shui," an additional fee) also became much more relaxed, only being ten cents. Finally, it even reached "bai hua" (no commission). The problem of head-lining (balancing accounts) has been resolved. However, in terms of dealing with draft tickets, people still chose to do business with reputable and reliable firms, otherwise, they would refuse. Therefore, the transaction volume remained low. Morning market transfers amounted to over 3.5 million, with new transactions of over 400,000. The afternoon market saw transactions of over 600,000, and transactions in the Small General Association amounted to over 300,000. As for the inflow and outflow of banknotes, due to the centralization of cash, everything was done with banknotes. Therefore, the amount collected back was only over 700,000, while the amount issued reached over 14.4 million. There were also exchanges of other silver coins and hard currency, which were not included as they were categorized under head commissions or remittance commissions and did not involve banknotes. As for the news about the bank's receiving prices, it was very simple yesterday. Because foreign exchange was all bought and sold by the central government, the inflows and outflows of various firms were all handled by the central government, so there were no inflows or outflows. The foreign banks' payments and receipts of drafts, various goods, remittance guarantees, telegram receipts, and other collections totaled 6.45 million. Due to the lack of cash, there were no inflows or outflows in warehousing. Chinese banks received and cleared drafts of over 3.2 million, and various goods, remittances, tax guarantees, and other collections amounted to 4.56 million. Japanese banks received and cleared drafts of over 2.2 million, various other collections of over 2.5 million, remittance transfers of only over 200,000, and telegraphic transfers of 400,000. Money houses received and cleared foreign public documents worth over 53.3 million and foreign head commissions of over 3.45 million, and remittances from various routes of over 300,000. Yesterday, the market announced that after the determination of various currency system allocations, increases or decreases were not allowed. Therefore, there were no quotations in the morning and afternoon markets yesterday, and the previous day's market allocations were followed. Both the Jiangnan and Guangdong subsidiary currencies were priced at 833.30 yuan, but transactions were completely off the books. Currently, the market rule is that 12 small silver dollars or 3,000 copper coins can be exchanged for one legal tender yuan, permanently fixed without fluctuation. Money houses, in such a situation where there is nothing to do and no profit to be made, disregarded everything and arbitrarily raised or lowered exchange rates, with some exchanging 400 cash for every ten cents of a silver dollar, some exchanging 300 cash for every ten cents, and copper coins ranging from 2,800 to 845 cash. Under these circumstances, ordinary residents suffered unnecessary losses. It is hoped that the government will have a solution to handle the aftermath.

American Cotton Lacks Distinctiveness Before Holiday 141

Yesterday, the American cotton market opened with quiet market conditions due to the upcoming holiday. Prices fell slightly due to cotton farmers' speculation and bullish profit-taking, with no frost damage reported, and down by one pound tone. Subsequently, prices rebounded as forecasts indicated frost in Oklahoma, Arkansas, and Texas tonight. Peers, Liverpool, and Japanese firms all bought in unison, absorbing all the speculative sales. Spring and Autumn

Vignettes 150

— (Xu Haowu)

Whether it's suicide, premature death, or a natural end: it's a heartfelt sorrow for flesh and blood, a wail over the coffin; or it's the removal of a thorn in one's side, allowing one to personally attend the funeral, feigning grief with joy, showing the deceased's intolerance and one's own greatness; or it's hiring "specialists" to "dutifully wear mourning," wailing loudly: the entire funeral hall is always filled with cries of anguish.

Death is always symbolized by the tears of bitterness, melancholy, and grief, uniformly painted with a desolate and tragic color.

In reality, no living thing can escape death. It is unnecessary to seek death when one is not destined to die; when one's time has come, as long as one's personality and career have had daily achievements, fulfilling the Creator's painstaking intention in giving body and mind, what is there to mourn in death, what is the bitterness of death?

A corpse lying still has its own silent, deeply meaningful charm. The masses, without serious introspection from this perspective, merely follow customs, wailing and being at a loss. Although there is the saying "the fox mourns the rabbit's death"; cold observation inevitably misses the bigger picture.

The Greatest Invention 151

— Pei Yu

If you were to ask several people what they consider the greatest invention from ancient times to the present, most would answer things like the steam engine, generator, or telegraph. But these are merely the results of earlier and more important inventions. The earliest and greatest human invention from ancient times to the present is the hammer.

Without a hammer, you cannot begin any small construction work. Although you may not directly use it in practice, the tools you use to work must be made with it. The hammer is the first tool that increased people's strength; it is difficult to accomplish anything with bare hands. The hammer was probably invented by an ancestor who was gifted with a divine power to use a stone to crack open the shell of an oyster or a whelk. The earliest hammers had no handle. It was just a stone, shaped for easy holding in the palm.

Attaching such a stone to a handle gives you a more effective tool. Chipping away one side of the stone that is frequently used to form a sharp edge transforms it into a stone axe. The creation of the cutting edge of the earliest flint tools relied entirely on a hammer. Such hammers gave rise to the earliest cutting tools, the axe and hand axe. From the hand axe and chisel to the saw is only one step. The drill is just a prototype chisel. It is the first thing with a round handle, rotated by the palm; later, primitive people invented the bow and made rope wrapped around the bow. Drills with bows and ropes are still used in some crafts today.

With a set of tools including hammers, axes, saws, and chisels, people can make huge logs into small pieces or long strips, and manufacture wheels or other circular objects. Every tool he made, and everything made with his tools, allowed his strength to control all other stronger forces in nature. Now there are several huge machines that can be started, stopped, accelerated, or decelerated with just the touch of a finger, and we can see the continuing effect of the combination of hammers, axes, saws, and chisels. So no matter what great, ingenious, and important things we might imagine will be invented, in the final analysis, we must give credit to the first person who used a stone to crack open an oyster.

A Country Brothel Madam 152

— Tianji

Mystery of Mystery? 153

— Yan Fusun

Since the rise of neon lights, slightly established stores have willingly undergone this modern baptism in order to decorate their storefronts. It is said that several large square characters can cost more than a thousand gold pieces. The store's consumption is taken from the customers, the wool comes from the sheep, which is understandable. What is most incomprehensible is the land deity's, that is, the west side of the New Shanghai Company on Nanjing Road (next to the old Shuanglong Tea Shop). Who spent a large sum of money to install a long neon light (about fifteen feet long and two feet wide), the electric current in the glass tube reflecting the six large characters "Namo Amitabha Buddha." Once dusk falls, the electric light shines directly, illuminating the city night, dazzling passersby. Someone estimated that such a grand decoration probably cost more than a thousand gold pieces. In the future, it will cost at least hundreds of dollars in electricity bills each month. Who is the anonymous great benefactor who secretly planted this virtuous deed? He sees that the world's morals are not what they used to be, and people's hearts are stealing day by day, so he specially erected this Buddha seat. He put on a set of modern clothes for him, and the electric light shot out can be regarded as the Buddha's light. Buddha's light shines everywhere, the earth is full of spring, and all the violent qi is transformed into auspiciousness and harmony. All the sins of the world are completely eliminated. Thus, his old man's goal is fully achieved. What does it matter if he spends a few dollars? However, this modern "neon" slogan, although relying on the boundless power of the Buddha and its own great radiance, can it ultimately penetrate Uncle Bao's heart? That is still a question—what is the meaning of this dense and bright light for life? Who can crack this mystery of mystery? Setting a new standard and creating an unprecedented spectacle, it stands tall in the metropolis of Shanghai, and at the center of Nanjing Road where it strikes the eye. This humorous Buddha light refuses to succumb and vanish. Is this mystery strange or not? It cannot be named, it is just mysterious!

The Ethereal Record of Imperial Incense 154

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

This situation was originally very common, because Prince Qing was the leader of the Grand Council, so he was often the first to report matters; but on this day, we saw the look on his face was really a bit different, although it cannot be said how different, it was just in our eyes, the same as when Li Yunying entered the palace earlier to report the flowering of the jade.

The Old Buddha naturally saw it very clearly, and her lips suddenly turned greyish-white.

She knew that the expected disaster had really come!

"What do you have to say?" she asked urgently, her tone very unnatural; although the other officials were all standing on both sides, the Empress Dowager seemed not to see them, staring at Prince Qing with all her attention, without turning her eyes for a moment.

"Returning to the Empress Dowager! This servant has just received some news," Prince Qing still revealed his usual demeanor of a high official, and reported in a low voice.

"What news? You should have reported it earlier!" The Empress Dowager was really very anxious, and couldn't help but say her own thoughts directly: "This morning, we had expected that there must be some bad news coming, and now you have indeed brought it!"

Although Prince Qing heard the Empress Dowager say this, and knew that the news he was about to report was indeed bad news, how could he deliberately deceive? So he plucked up his courage and replied:

"Japan has declared war on Russia!" (452)

The Space-Shrinking Technique of Returning to Jingzhou 155

— (Pan)

Now, anyone with a little geographical knowledge knows that going from Nanjing to Jingzhou requires passing through the four provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei. Even going to Jiujiang, how much of a journey is that? During the Three Kingdoms period, there were probably no unobstructed highways! How is it that in the play of Liu Bei returning to Jingzhou, starting from Nanjing, he escaped Zhou Yu's garrison at Chisang Pass in just one day? Even if we consider that he was riding a steed that could travel a thousand miles a day, and that he had the ability to leap over streams, so that even places where the water was cut off would not hinder his galloping, yet Madam Sun was clearly sitting in a carriage pulled by manpower, could it be that there was also divine help in secret? I think that although place names may have changed from ancient times to the present, the land itself would not shrink, would it?

Little Western Paradise 156

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 21: Gently, She Showed Maternal Affection in the Courtyard, and Angrily, She Reproached Her Son-in-Law with a Lion's Roar from the Next Room

Fortunately, my father had gone to the army, and he was still in our fort, so I could see him every day, and I wasn't too sad at first. One morning, the army suddenly left, taking my father with them. Everyone in the fort was overjoyed, feeling a burden lifted, but only my family cried our hearts out. From then on, we didn't get any news of my father. Later, after two years, a villager from a nearby village, who had been in the same camp as my father, escaped home and told us that my father had died in battle half a year ago. The three women in my family suffered and struggled through these years. When we thought about the future, and that there would be no day of relief, we disregarded our lives and came to Xi'an. Unexpectedly, when we got to Xi'an, I ended up like this. As she spoke, she began to shed tears. Old Mrs. Zhu said: On the way here, I heard people say that when you get to Xi'an, you've reached paradise, and you don't have to worry about anything. When we got here, we saw that paradise is indeed paradise, but it's paradise for the rich, not paradise for the poor. Inside Little Western Paradise, everything is good, but for us poor people, looking at the back door, we can't even get in. Mrs. Zhou laughed: You see this place as paradise, but some people see it as hell. But if I say this to you, you wouldn't believe it. Mrs. Jia, you've lived in Little Western Paradise for a few days now, do you think this is paradise or hell? (356)

Travel Notes

Footprints on the Lake 157

— Lü Mengjiao

A Night at Nanping

Three days after the Double Ninth Festival in the year Yihai, I had business in Wulin and hurried back to the lake. In the evening, I drove my car to Jingci Temple, where the monks Ruopiao and Wanyuan came out to greet me upon hearing the sound. After tea, we set up wine and sat in the Jingye Courtyard, drinking heartily. There were many playful words in the conversation. Laughter often reached outside the door. There was no meat in the temple, so I brought out the dried meat and smoked fish slices that I had brought with me to accompany the wine, which tasted very good. I remembered that I had stayed in temples three times in my life, namely Wannian Temple, Zhongfang Guang Temple, and Tiantong Temple, and this was the fourth, but I was much happier here. At that time, all the monks were asleep, and I heard no human voices. The cool moon peeked through the window, and the severe frost was on the ground. I heard autumn insects chirping on all four walls like rain, and I felt as if I was in a dream.

Foggy Lake

At dawn, I heard the bell of Nanping Temple ringing slowly, so I put on my clothes and went out of the temple, and went boating on the lake with Master Fen, Meng Qi, and Ruopiao. The morning fog was thick, misty like a curtain. Looking into the distance, the twin peaks of Ge Ling had disappeared, but the Six Bridges and Two Pools sometimes appeared and disappeared. The lake surface was covered by water vapor, floating and illusionary, and uncertainly hidden and revealed. Leaving Baiyun Nunnery, the fog became heavier, and my clothes felt damp. Looking around, the boat seemed to be floating in the vast sea, so I asked the boatman to put down the oars and sing wildly, no longer knowing what world I was in. I then said to the fellow travelers: "Today's tour is really far from the mundane world, so why bother to take a raft?" Everyone was very happy. After a while, the fog stopped, the sun came out, and the light was bright and warm, so we returned from Xiaoyingzhou, drumming our oars. People say that the scenery of West Lake, a sunny lake is not as good as a rainy lake, but I say that a rainy lake is not as good as a foggy lake. A rainy lake is wonderful, but a foggy lake is even more wonderful.

Exploring Osmanthus in Manjuelong

Osmanthus is distinguished by color, with gold osmanthus and silver osmanthus. By time, there is early osmanthus and late osmanthus. In the past, the osmanthus markets of West Lake were mostly in Lingyin and Three Tianzhu, and the New Southern Book records: "There are many osmanthus trees in Lingyin Mountain in Hangzhou, and the monks call them moon osmanthus. Often one falls on the Mid-Autumn Festival night." Also, the Group of Fragrant Plants says: "Mountain osmanthus is most abundant in Tianzhu, and the monks call it moon osmanthus, and its flowers are often continuous, with a few spots vaguely on the branches and under the leaves, which is also a different species." Now, Manjuelong is the most prosperous, with all kinds of osmanthus, and you can count the flowers in autumn. When the flowers bloom, the sea is golden and the waves are silver, and the fragrance covers several miles. People come from all directions to explore, shoulder to shoulder. The residents often place tables and chairs under the trees for the viewers to sit and rest, and the income they receive each season is quite large. When the autumn colors are at their peak, I take two or three poet friends to explore the osmanthus. I hired a rickshaw from Jingci Temple, six miles, to the foot of Wengjia Mountain. The slopes gradually became higher, and the rickshaw swayed and could not go up, so I took off my leather shoes, put on monk shoes, and walked with a staff. When I arrived at Manjuelong, the late osmanthus had already withered. Tables and chairs were scattered among the trees, silver petals were strewn everywhere, and the remaining fragrance still lingered on my clothes. I called for a palanquin carrier around noon, passed Shuile Cave, and listened to the clear sound of the spring, with a natural rhythm, and finally felt refreshed.

Dragon Well

After the revolution, West Lake has also changed its state several times. The embankment is getting wider day by day, and the lake surface is getting narrower day by day. Who knows if it will not become farmland in the future? This is something to worry about for Xizi. Recently, many wealthy merchants like to occupy a seat in West Lake to be honored, with buildings lined up and more houses than mountains. Those who claim to be elegant are actually tarnishing the lake and mountains. I say that today's tourists to West Lake, what they see are only foreign buildings and foreign consulates, and what they hear are the sounds of cars and machines, with all kinds of noises, and the quiet state is lost. Is it still possible to seek the past, when one could ride a donkey and wander among the smoke and willows of Banqiao? All my fellow travelers had the same feeling, so we decided to seek a place deep in the mountains and rivers, which would only be Fengyu Ridge, Jiuxi, and Lian'an. It was decided. Traveling east from Santai Mountain, the noise gradually disappeared, and my mood was refreshed. Passing Ling Shi Mountain, I looked at the mountains surrounded by the inside, the towering cliffs and deep ravines. Doves cooed in the empty mountains, and floating clouds gathered from all directions, with the intention of rain. Entering Fengyu Ridge, the yellow leaves beside the road rustled, and the green bamboo swayed, all with a desolate and clear feeling. Reaching the Two Old Men Pavilion, the rain came. The smoke and clouds over the lake were swirling, and the scenery was incredibly beautiful. Looking back at Hugong Ridge, the setting sun and the Wu Palace were all submerged in the fog. I wanted to cross Yanhua Ridge and visit Jiuxi Lian'an, but was prevented by the rain. So I huddled with Shi Zishu Fan and Prince Tie Hua on the pavilion. Listening quietly to the boiling tea in the pine tripod, my heart was relaxed and content, as if I had gained something. After noon, the weather cleared, and I returned from Maojiabu to visit Yue's Tomb. I ascended to the Qingyuan Wine House for a little drink, savoring the pleasure of this tour, and unknowingly got drunk.

Treatment of Gonorrhea 158

— Dr. Yuan Yimin

To discuss the treatment methods for gonorrhea, it's necessary to briefly explain what kind of disease it is and its condition. Only then can we understand which methods are reasonable and which are not. The first time you get gonorrhea, it is mostly acute anterior urethral gonorrhea, with very few exceptions. Anterior urethral gonorrhea refers to the fact that gonorrhea bacteria only attack and multiply in the anterior part of the urethra. Logically, local symptoms only require local treatment, and drugs to kill gonorrhea bacteria are readily available everywhere. Why do Chinese and foreign doctors consider it a difficult disease to treat? Because the gonorrhea bacteria are lurking in the inner layer of the urethral mucosa. If you want to completely kill the gonorrhea bacteria without damaging the mucosa at all, it is difficult under such narrow circumstances. However, if you can apply it skillfully, you can recover completely. There are many methods for treating gonorrhea, including electrotherapy, washing, injection, and internal medicine. Electrotherapy uses hyperthermia, which is divided into long-wave and short-wave. Long-wave therapy must be applied close to the body, which is not only troublesome but also has many disadvantages, with the risk of burning the skin and little effect. In recent times, the most popular method is short-wave diathermy, which can be treated through clothing and is effective quickly. Using the light power of electrical equipment to kill bacteria, the best one is the latest turbidimeter. The light power of this machine can penetrate deep into the skin without any damage. Washing and injecting involves injecting a sterilizing liquid into the urethra. The distribution of the washing liquid according to the condition, the concentration used, and the time are all related. Nowadays, the injection of gonorrhea serum is more appreciated. The best preparation of this kind is "Gono-Serol." Injection is giving a shot. Yellow pigment and mixed gonorrhea vaccine have a certain status in treatment. Yellow pigment can penetrate the membrane and kill bacteria, and mixed gonorrhea bacteria can make the body produce antibacterial bodies, thereby achieving the purpose of eliminating bacteria. Among these preparations, the better ones include Antiseptine Trypaflavine. Internal medicine focuses on strong pain relief, anti-inflammatory, and bactericidal power, with those that can disinfect the urinary tract and penetrate deep into the mucosa being superior. It is important to avoid those that contain strong astringent ingredients. The current sterilization drug used by doctors is quite suitable and is an excellent preparation. Although the treatment of gonorrhea is as mentioned above, diseases change in myriad ways and cannot be generalized. Moreover, the treatment of gonorrhea, even with a slight difference, can leave endless harm, such as prolonging the recovery period and developing into chronic diseases. These are all the results of wrong methods and random medication. The Chunzai Hospital at 66 Ningbo Road, French Concession, this city, is presided over by Mr. Feng Shanliang, a famous doctor at sea. The hospital's treatment of gonorrhea, the novelty of the methods, and the skill of the methods can be said to be second to none. Other equipment such as electrical equipment is complete, and it has reached the pinnacle of gonorrhea treatment.

Talk

The Weather is Fine, the Sun is Out 167

— Xu Xizhen

When I was little, I went to variety shows and enjoyed listening to Shanghai opera. I was most fond of the clowns who would interject comical remarks. Especially when they sat in the center, solemnly shaking their broken fans and starting with the opening line: "Ah han! The weather is fine, the sun is out! The rain wets the steps." At the time, I didn't understand the ways of the world, or things like humor, but looking at those "serious-looking" funny faces, I found it quite interesting. However, thinking about it now, I find it almost pitiful.

The reason why clowns are so popular in plays is first and foremost because they are considerate and don't offend anyone. Whether it's the superiors or inferiors, left or right, big or small, when they make a funny face for you and add a "Yes, sir! How do you do?", it's much more welcome than a lengthy speech of "righteous opinion." Secondly, clowns' speech also requires some skill. This "skill" doesn't mean they say anything profound, but rather that they talk and talk, and in the end, it's as if they said nothing at all. In a society full of traps, this kind of skill is necessary. Modern people don't find it easy to speak. And "eat more, talk less" is an ancient Chinese saying. However, humans are truly strange creatures; it's not easy to keep one's mouth shut and say nothing, but as soon as one opens one's mouth, the crisis of "trouble comes from the mouth" follows you. As a last resort, thinking from a small perspective and considering the grand cause of "universal peace," some people have come out to advocate "talking about foxes and ghosts, discussing flies," etc. But even though foxes and ghosts are vague, and flies are tiny, in the end, there's still something there. If you greet people with "The weather is good today" like in the old days, that's even more inappropriate. First, this statement has too much critical coloring; you might say the weather is good because you got paid, while I insist on saying the weather is bad because you wouldn't understand my state of mind. That is to say, maybe it's because I was just turned down for a loan. Subjective criticism is unacceptable, and objective criticism is "please don't speak your mind," so in addition to "talking about foxes and ghosts, discussing flies," there's the clownish "the weather is fine, the sun is out, the rain wets the steps," a way of speaking.

It is said that the past year was a "year of humor," and what kind of year this year is is uncertain, but judging by the situation, the life philosophy of "the weather is fine, the sun is out" is probably still not outdated, and the clown's act is not yet disliked by people. Then, this year might be the "year of the clown" when the clown is in the spotlight.

After all, the world has reached the end of the night, and it really should be "the weather is fine, the sun is out."

Road 168

— Luo Zhihua

I stopped in front of a small door near the city wall. I tapped on the newly painted black gate, and someone inside responded. At the same time, a woman's head appeared at the small window next to the door. I told her my name. After a short while, the sound of leather shoes hitting the stone slabs echoed, and I knew that Dong was coming out. Because that footstep was very familiar to me. When the door opened with a creak, his forever-smiling face was once again in front of me.

His study was a small room. Although it was just five o'clock in the afternoon, darkness had already enveloped it. After he let me sit on a chair without a back, I couldn't say the few words I had prepared. What was wrong? He didn't show any sign of rejecting my conversation, and he wouldn't dislike my conversation either. But I couldn't say it.

——How's life? Long time no see.

I said that after a long period of deliberation. I don't know how many times I've said these kinds of things. It always starts like this every time we meet. The reason is that I'm often whipped so painfully by life that I can't even lift my head. For others, I think the same - a person living in this era is full of depression everywhere! He still replied to me like a smiling Buddha:

——It's okay, it's okay!

He handed me a glass of plain water. I drank it, surveying the layout of the room. It was still clean, but the walls had lost their vitality due to age. On this old wall, there was a central hanging scroll and two couplets.

His eyes followed mine, surveying the scene.

My actions were like those of a stranger who had just arrived. Did he doubt me? He asked me how life was. My answer took a long time to come out, and it was the words I had prepared. I truthfully told him about my suffering in life, as well as other things. The most important thing was that I wanted to borrow some money from him.

It was very clear that he didn't have money either; but, he still had a home. As for me, I didn't have a home, no friends, no, I had one, and that was Dong.

He put away his forever-smiling face, and replaced it with an enthusiastic expression seized by deep affection. He extended the hand that always holds people tightly, to me, expressing sincere apology.

——You should know me, there's no way my family can provide me with money (lowering his voice to say:) Father only knows how to smoke opium, Mother only knows how to save money. There's no way I can get any money. It's really…

His two hands rubbed together, as if he was too apologetic.

Then, we shifted to other topics.

Probably his father had returned. The sound of conversation from the house across the way could often be heard, along with the scent of opium.

As I was about to leave, I happened to run into him walking toward this house. I followed him back to where we had been originally. This was his idea, he wanted to say a few words with me. While we were talking, his hand held a shiny white copper water pipe, taking puffs with a creaking sound. First, he asked me about Dong's affairs at school, and also asked about mine, before uttering his opinion:

——I still don't approve of this Western school. Don't look at how fashionable his mother is… Look at what Dong has become, even getting married (author's note: marriage) he objects to!… Objections? If he objects, I won't let him go to school, and we'll see about paying tuition after the summer vacation!

"Suddenly," he blew away a pile of ash.

Dong stood blankly by the bed, his legs leaning against the edge of the bed. His eyes were constantly staring at the ceiling or the damp ground. He also looked at me as if many worries were piled on him. As for me, I was like a co-judge, feeling amused and sad. His father walked out without expressing anything to anyone. I comforted him and walked out of that black lacquer door with an empty stomach.

Comforting myself, how grateful I am to not have the burden of a family or relatives, but where should I go? My stomach is hungry, my clothes are torn, how will I maintain my life tomorrow or today?

Sedan Chairs and Rickshaws 169

— Yan

Small Chronicle of a Village Trip

The train pulled into Waiyangqi. I looked out the window towards the station. Outside the wooden fence, on both sides of the road, the former black, dovecote-like sedan chairs had been completely replaced by rickshaws. No, it would be more accurate to say they had been replaced by rickshaws.

In the past, sedan chairs were the only means of transportation in my hometown. Sedan chair businesses did not stop anywhere like streetcars; they had fixed storefronts, like rickshaw stations in Japan. Moreover, the cost of a sedan chair was quite high, unaffordable for the average person, more than ten times higher than in places like Hangzhou where mountain sedan chairs cost one or two yuan per day. In my hometown's county town, which was only three li across, the cost was no less than one yuan. Therefore, the sedan chair business was very bleak. However, visiting guests, attending banquets, especially year-end gratitude ceremonies and New Year's greetings at mansions were always done in sedan chairs to enhance appearances. As long as a sedan chair business had a few contracted mansions, they had nothing to fear.

As for the organization of sedan chair businesses: some were run by the owner, who provided several sedan chairs and hired sedan chair carriers, paying them a fixed monthly salary. Very few operated on a profit-sharing basis. Others were owned by a few people who provided the sedan chairs; they were all bosses and shared the business equally. The latter was more profitable because expenses were lower and they took the business seriously. Although they didn't have guild rules, the boundaries were very clear. If a certain sedan chair business or group of people had a business arrangement with a certain mansion, they would never try to snatch it unless there were special circumstances. When going to a sedan chair business to hire a sedan chair, as long as you recognized the servant who worked at a certain mansion, even if the sedan chair carrier who usually did business with that family wasn't at the shop, his companions would find a way to call them. The reason they didn't interfere with each other was naturally because the income was good. The sedan chair carriers would spend their time chatting and playing cards in teahouses near the sedan chair business. In the second and third months of the year, after the New Year's business was done, the sedan chair carriers would gamble quite a bit of money.

Few mansions had their own sedan chairs. Those who did had either served as minor officials or had considerable status. The former wanted to put on airs, and the sedan chair was often inherited from the past. As long as they regularly hired two sedan chair carriers at home, who also had兼職，呼喝過市的時候總覺較轎行里叫來的威嚇，—這近乎上海洋車和包車的　別。後者必是鄉紳之類，他們公事多，進出忙，自備籘轎旣便利，開消又省。這兩種籘轎，在街上路人大都認得出是某家的。第三種輪到太夫了，（故鄉從前是沒有醫生的）他們不但自備籘轎，轎夫更由兩名而增至三名。普通籘轎以安步當車為漂亮，坐轎的人撫着轎前的　手板，身體微微向前，頭部探出在轎門之外，遇到熟人，互相招呼，態度是莊嚴而自然。　夫的籘轎就不　，一個轎夫在前面開道，嘴里高聲吆喝着，招呼　人讓路，後面兩名轎夫就健步　　　追隨着，那大夫坐在轎里就　得十分得意了。他們的意思是看病如救火，要愈快愈好；至於用三名轎夫，那表示這大夫的出診忙，兩名轎夫恐怕沒有休息的時候，就　備一名作為預備軍了。寫到這裏，我記起一個笑話，而且是實事，故鄉的父老輩大都能夠詳詳細細講述的。在若干年前，一位大夫掛牌之後，沒有生意，他就異想天開發明了坐籘轎的廣告術，他每天坐了籘轎，大街小巷亂跑，以示他的忙於診務。但是故鄉地面小，他的籘轎祗見滿街飛，却不見在人家門前停歇，他的西洋鏡終於穿拆了。

自從三年前故鄉的建設局拆平橋樑，修築馬路之後，不知怎樣一來，通行洋車了。洋車通行之後，自然轎行都受了打擊，紛紛倒閉。起初由人包辦洋車一百輛，劃定了多少站頭，大有求過於供的樣子。拉車子的人就是由哪些轎夫改行的，他們雖然覺得沒有做轎夫時的舒服，進欵却增加。因為籘轎是要二人分拆的，洋車就獨自進益，定價比籘轎賤，坐的人就多，車租是論月的，自然比之上海論日的要便宜許多。這樣，一般農忙過後的莊稼人，及每日徘徊於茶館的小販，都想來搶吃這碗飯了。利之所在，人皆爭之，包辦洋車的亦分頭鑚營，於是××洋車行××洋車行都開起來，車輛由一百二百而五百，現在馬路兩旁的兩列洋車，像金蒼蠅似的不知有多少輛了。

火車駛進站，車廂是吐出寥寥的幾個乘客，但是走到木柵收票處，團團的被車夫圍上了：叫着，喊着，你幾乎懷疑在什麽碼頭上岸，一不留意，或許你的行李已被人搶去了，不過這是搶生意，祗要必去坐上他的車，什麽都不會短少的。如果有兩隻手搶着你的行李時，那就得費一番周折了，因為他們有的是功夫，能夠許久堅持着不放手，你這個行李的主人就祗有站着等他們分勝負。

Red Smartweed 170

— Jing Jia

When mentioning flowers of autumn, everyone will think of chrysanthemums. But I think that the loveliness of chrysanthemums is far inferior to that of red smartweed.

Chrysanthemums are indeed lovely in some ways. For example, chrysanthemums do not bloom in the spring when all flowers are competing for beauty, nor in the summer when it is easy to survive, but bloom when frost and snow are about to impose their power on all things. This point is indeed a commendable advantage of chrysanthemums. In addition, the posture, color, and fragrance of chrysanthemums are enough to give people a pleasant mood and have been cherished.

However, the loveliness of red smartweed is no less than that of chrysanthemums. Although she does not have the gorgeous flowers of chrysanthemums, and she does not have the dazzling colors of chrysanthemums, her graceful and charming posture, and her red and white, slender and exquisite flowers can also bring joy.

Not only that, red smartweed has another value that is more precious than chrysanthemums. When we see chrysanthemums, we seem to see a modern urban girl cultivated in rouge and powder, while red smartweed is like a healthy and beautiful girl living in the countryside. The former will pretend to be charming, forcing people to love them; the latter can use her innate nature, truthfully and genuinely, to move people naturally. Forced love is false, and natural emotion is pure.

Although red smartweed has this kind of loveliness, it is ignored. She is not cultivated in delicate flower pots, nor is she worshiped on elegant tables. No beauty wears her in her hair, and no one holds appreciation meetings for her. People have only apathetic attitudes toward her. Therefore, she can only hide in the corners of ponds and riversides, accompanying the lonely geese that have lost their flocks, and sobbing with the autumn wind.

However, this may be the luck of red smartweed, that she can maintain her natural nature in the natural world. Even if this is not her luck, it is not worth our pity. Isn't everything in the world like this? The false and pretentious are supported by people, while the genuine and natural are buried among the grass and trees.

STORYTELLING 174

Xia Hesheng's Three Smiles

Dunben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "Night of the Tang Palace"

The moon wheel is high before the Hall of Eternal Life. Red candles burn incense in the ninth heaven. A full plate of fruits is offered in the courtyard. Jade flutes play Phoenix Xiao in unison. Look at a bay of new moon water. Autumn is so wonderfully clever. The autumn wind brushes the face, and excitement is doubled. Looking back at the Milky Way filling the magpie bridge. The heavenly maiden smiles faintly, waving her hand to the Cowherd across the river. Although the Double Seventh Festival happens every year, we chat about it once a year. Yang Guifei kneels on a brocade futon, slowly adding fragrant droplets. Under the double moon, first, I wish the country will always be united, and the smoke of war will be extinguished to avoid gunfire. Second, I wish the emperor good health, and a life as long as Mount Tai. Third, I wish the concubine Yang to always be by the Western Palace, enjoying the emperor's favor. Morning and evening, I attend the emperor, never separating in life and sharing the same path in death. Only then did the concubine express her heartfelt intentions.

Xing Ruiting's Hairpin Phoenix

Huiling (1380) 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Manchu Opening

The north wind howls, rolling up yellow sand. North of the border are all Manchu families. Running horses and shooting arrows are the heroes. (There is) a second young lady born with the beauty of a flower. (Born with) a melon-seed face like a hibiscus. A hibiscus face (born with) willow-leaf eyebrows and bright autumn eyes. A powder-white nose like jade. A small cherry mouth. Glutinous rice silver teeth. A large ring flower is inserted high beside her ear. Wearing a black gauze hood. (Also) a bright pearl radiating light. Wearing a long cheongsam. (Wearing) a 'da la la' style of embroidered shoes. A 'da la la' style of embroidered shoes. Embroidered with flower patterns all over the vamp. The young lady is alone and bored. To pass the time, she plays the pipa. First, she plays a song of Xiangfei's Grievance. Then, she caresses the lonely wild goose landing on the sandy shore. Then, she plays a song of General's Order. General's Order. (Only) Zhong Ziqi can meet Yu Boya. The young lady is playing the pipa. Playing the pipa. (Suddenly) a handsome trouble-maker arrives. The trouble-maker is only seventeen or eighteen years old. Snow-white face. (Without) a single pockmark. Wearing a long arrow-sleeved coat and a short jacket. Wearing a melon-skin cap. Hanging a tobacco pouch on his waist. His left hand is holding a small child. His right hand is leading a piebald mule. The young lady immediately stands up. Calling out, "Brother, please sit down." (Waiting for) little sister to send you a cup of milk tea. (That trouble-maker) seeing that the great king is not at home. Says, "Let's play together." The two of them fall drunkenly on Yang Guifei's couch… An old mama runs in from outside. Eighty-eight years old. Head full of white hair. Holding a dragon-head cane. Says, "You two young rascals. What are you doing here in broad daylight? The old king. Is coming back. He's going to. Cut off your heads." Laughing. Haha, hee hee, haha. The young lady reaches out and slaps her hard across the mouth. Cursing, "Old rascal. Is coming back. I'm not afraid of him. Killing a head. A bowl-sized scar." Saying. "Wu li bi. Wu li ya. Wu li men deng bei'er cha. Zhi cha ya. Zhi ya cha. Wu li zhi ge da. Ge da bei'er ya." Speaking foreign words. Speaking barbarian talk. We Chinese. How would we understand him?

The repair department attached to the Wufunong intersection of Nanjing Road (Siming Savings Association) is managed by the association's specialized and knowledgeable engineers. They usually repair radios with outstanding results and are highly praised by all sectors. Recently, in order to expand the repair department, the association has opened a large-scale repair workshop and newly imported precision instruments from abroad to inspect and repair various sound machines. The repair fee is low, the delivery is fast, and satisfaction is guaranteed after repair. The association is now planning to repair damaged radios for those who have them, so you can call 933626, and someone will be sent to inspect and repair them.

LIANHUA HEADLINES 177

In recent months, the intense work at the Lianhua Photography Studio has been quite astonishing. Sets are everywhere, the sound of the camera is heard everywhere, the lights are on all night, and shadows are looming. In the current depressed film industry, the spirit of Lianhua colleagues who are working so hard is truly comforting to the people of the country.

Since the announcement that "Tianlun" will be performed, it has aroused great attention across the country. According to the outstanding achievements of this film in various aspects, it is truly a credit to the Chinese film industry. All national music dubbing has been completed, and the performance date is near.

Sun Yu's new work "Go to Nature" has yielded unexpectedly satisfactory results in Qingdao's outdoor scenes. The interior scenes are being set up and can be filmed soon.

Wang Hanlun has begun working on "Crying Remnants of Red." Her expression is mature and extraordinary. Many who visited the set praised her.

"Three Modern Men" has begun filming.

After "Four Sisters," Yang Xiaozhong is working on the script for "Wildcat." It is now halfway done. It is planned that Wang Renmei will star in this film. A wildcat starring in "Wildcat" is also a good story in the film industry.

Xu Jian, the wildcat type, often comes to the factory with Li Lili, Lu Lu, and others to play ball. Xu is as light as a swallow, and her jumping posture is extremely beautiful. Yan Yan constantly applauds and cheers.

Ge Zuozhi plays a lonely and helpless wanderer in "Lost Lamb." The other day, during the filming of the night of wind and rain, Xiao Ge was wandering the streets like a chicken that had fallen into the water, in a very miserable state.

Hong Jingling, who never plays good people, has recently been selected to play the eldest son in "Song of a慈母 (Címǔ - Loving Mother)." Jin Yan, Zheng Junli, and others play his younger brothers. But this elder brother is not a good person either.

Chen Yanyan plays a singer in her recent work "Crying Remnants of Red," wearing a floral dress and a headscarf, holding a pipa, smiling quietly, walking lightly, with the style of an ancient beauty.

Shen Bao Local Supplement, Automobile Weekly

THE BIRTH OF THE DIESEL BUS 181

— Wu

Cummins High-Speed ​​Diesel Engine Company's attempt to manufacture a diesel engine bus has recently been successful. Therefore, the honor of creating the first production record belongs to the company and its director, Cummins. According to this bus, it is made by using the Auburn eight-cylinder chassis. Except for the diesel engine. Everything else remains the same. That is, the installation location of the engine. There is no slightest change. As for the price of the product and its sales plan. Nothing has been heard so far.

Fuel saving. On the day the news was released, Mr. Cummins personally drove his first product. Drive straight from New York to the Pacific coast. Make an economic journey. It is expected that the fuel required for this trip. Should not exceed eight US dollars. The heavy oil used by the engine. It is very convenient to purchase. Because villagers use oil-fired machines. It's all there is. Oil prices vary by region. From 3 cents to 1 dime US dollars per gallon. The average price is about 6 cents US dollars. However, there are places where national taxes must be added. Its selling price will be higher than this. Ordinary users. Each gallon can travel 40 to 50 miles. The degree of fuel consumption. Depends on the speed.

The speed increases sharply. Mr. Cummins's faith in the diesel bus. It hasn't changed for years. Now that the effort has been successful, the bus manufacturing industry has gained a new field. Is it only Mr. Cummins's proposition that can be implemented. The history of Cummins Company manufacturing diesel engines. It dates back to 1919. The initial products. Only for stationary and marine diesel engines. Later, diesel engines for trucks, buses and rail vehicles. They were released one after another. Today, let's take the diesel engine for trucks as an example. Those used by people. The number reaches more than 1,000 units.

In March 1930. Mr. Cummins installed a Cummins marine diesel engine on a four-cylinder Packard car in Daytona. Created a speed of 80.398 miles per hour. Created the first official record for diesel engines. Attracted the attention of the world. In 1931, he returned to Daytona. Created a new record of 100.75 miles per hour. By the beginning of this year. Biel Cummins broke all records in Daytona. And created the highest diesel speed of 137.199 miles per hour. Those who participated in the Indianapolis car race. In 1931, there was Mr. Evans. At a speed of 86.170 miles per hour. Ranked thirteenth. In 1924, the late Mr. Sott Steburfel also reached the peak. At a speed of 88.566 miles per hour. Ranked twelfth. The cars used by these two people. All are equipped with Cummins diesel engines.

Not very flexible. This time Mr. Cummins made a trip across the United States. The reporter accompanied the end seat. It is also driving the section of road within the boundary of Virginia. From Lexington to White Sulphur Springs. Measuring 72 miles long. It was found that this high-pressure engine is not as flexible as a gasoline engine. Even its power is smaller. Although the direct transmission of the high gear ratio is changed to a ratio of 4.000 to 1. The centrifugal transmission is changed to a ratio of 2.65 to 1. Still cannot compete with the power of Auburn. Standard tooth rate. The former is 4.30. The latter is 3.20. The maximum speed of the car. Not enough time to calculate. However, it is more than enough to travel 65 miles per hour. Standing behind the car. You can often smell a gas. In the car. The slightest feeling is not felt.

The engine is a six-cylinder overhead valve type. Has a long push rod to raise and lower the valve and piston pin. Its bore and stroke are 3.75 and 5 inches. The piston displacement is 331 cubic inches. It is said to produce 85 horsepower. Its speed is 2,200 revolutions per minute. The original engine used by Auburn. Its horsepower is also 85 horsepower. But its speed is 3,500 revolutions per minute.

Weight reduction. Diesel engines are considered heavy. But the total weight of the Cummins Diesel engine. Only 860 pounds. Only 80 pounds heavier than the gasoline engine of the Auburn eight-cylinder car. The reason for its lightness. There are about two points. Once the design is meticulous. One is the change in the cylinder head and cylinder head. Aluminum alloy is the one. The movable cylinder is connected. Then it is made of cast iron. If the cast iron outside the speed limiter and injector can be changed to aluminum alloy. Then it can reduce the weight by 20 to 30 pounds again.

We hope that the weight of the diesel engine can be reduced to the same as that of the gasoline engine. It is not impossible to achieve this goal. However, it is important to know that. Although its speed is lower. But its piston displacement is even larger than Auburn's 279,9 cubic inches. It is 331,4 cubic inches. Therefore, the reason why Cummins's total vehicle weight is 250 pounds heavier than the original Auburn car. Because it needs to be equipped with a large starter. Batteries. And generators are the biggest reasons.

Requires a powerful starter. This diesel engine has a compression force of 500 pounds. Therefore, a powerful starter is required. Therefore, its batteries and engine. I also had to use a heavy one. The entire mechanism is operated with 12 volts. The generator is 225 watts. Several times larger than those used in other buses. The piston is made of aluminum alloy.

Another message. According to news released in Indianapolis. The first batch of buses equipped with diesel engines in the United States. Can be sold in a few months. This vehicle. Produced by Court Automobile Company. It is a diesel engine manufactured by Columbus City Cummins Machine Company and installed on an Auburn car body. As to whether it is still enough to promote abroad. Still not known. The provinces where diesel engines are used are well recognized. But at present, whether this engine can be applied to buses. Then the language is different. Each insists on a national language. Initially, I didn’t expect the Court Company to actually start proceeding in the midst of disputes. However, according to the recent opinions of Mr. Sloan, Vice President of General Motors. It is said that the engine is currently unusable in passenger cars.

ZHEBEI AUTOMOBILE TRAVELOGUE (LOWER) 182

— Ling Yun

On Sunday morning at 8:45, I departed from Hangzhou, planning to cross the Qiantang River, four miles away from Hangzhou, but soon encountered the third obstacle, because it was reported that the bridge across the river had been interrupted. This kind of news was surprising to me, because I had inquired from the China Travel Service and the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau this morning whether this route could be used or not. I returned to Hangzhou and left the Wulinmen Station at 10:00 a.m. The speedometer was 5.255 miles. With Tianmu Mountain as the destination, I departed from the station and proceeded along the avenue passing through Changhua to Huizhou. After traveling 30 miles, I saw an ancient stone bridge spanning the clear stream. The scenery was very good and worth a visit. After following the stream in the shade of old trees, I set off for Lin'an at 11:30 a.m. The mileage record of the speedometer was 5,288 miles. At 12:15 p.m., I saw a fork in the mountain road in front of me. From Wulinmen Station to here, the journey was 48 miles. I turned the rudder to the right and entered the branch road for 12 miles, passing through a mountain path with excellent scenery, and arrived at a station. Travelers can abandon the car and walk about half a mile to reach the Tianmao Hotel at the foot of the mountain. Its location is in the valley at the foot of Tianmu Mountain, which is very quiet. This hotel is being renamed Tianmu Mountain Hotel. The equipment inside is very modern. It is not very far from Shanghai. For those who like the quiet of mountain living, the melodious sound of clear springs, and mountaineering, this place is really the best place to rest. The hotel also offers a 10% discount to all members of the Chinese Automobile Club.

I encountered the first rain of this trip in the mountains. The misty veil shrouded the mountain scenery. Otherwise, the mountain is more than 4,000 feet high, and looking up and down, there is enough to please the eye. The characteristic of Tianmu Mountain, in addition to fir trees and strange trees, is also full of bamboo groves, which is quite different from the mountains seen along the way. After climbing for two hours from the foot of the mountain, I reached the temple on the top of the mountain. The scenery along the way is worth a visit. Those who are not physically strong can hire a mountain sedan to travel, which is very comfortable.

My initial travel destination was to reach Huangshan via the Qiantang River, and then to Yandang Mountain via Wenzhou. Unfortunately, due to obstacles in the middle, I could not follow the original plan, so I stayed at Tianqieshan for another day and a half. On Wednesday morning at 10:45 a.m., I left the bus station near Tianmu Mountain and arrived in the suburbs of Hangzhou at an average speed of 27 miles per hour. The record on the speedometer was 5,367 miles. The Wulinmen bus station arrived at 12:30 p.m. The mileage was 5.373 miles. When using the 50th gallon of gasoline, I left Hangzhou for Shanghai, a journey of 133 miles. Except for a 40-minute break in the middle, I arrived in Shanghai at 5:30 p.m. Those who want to travel by car in Zhejiang Province should pay attention to the fact that when this article was written, the Qianjiang Nandu Bridge across the Qiantang River in southern Zhejiang was interrupted and cars could not pass. The road south of Yuxi was also washed away by the water, and the road from western Zhejiang to Anhui was also impassable due to collapse. The location is 17 miles from the other end of Chun'an.
